## Overview

Mor Khazgur Mine

**Mor Khazgur Mine** is a small [orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum "Skyrim:Orichalcum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") supporting the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"). It contains only one zone, *[Mor Khazgur Mine](#Mor_Khazgur_Mine)*.

It is owned and worked by [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") from Mor Khazgur. [Shuftharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Shuftharz "Skyrim:Shuftharz") will [buy orichalcum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ghamorz](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghamorz "Skyrim:Ghamorz")  [Gul](/wiki/Skyrim:Gul "Skyrim:Gul")  [Olur](/wiki/Skyrim:Olur "Skyrim:Olur") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The exterior of the mine is the Orc stronghold of Mor Khazgur. The path leading up to the entrance passes the stronghold's [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") on the left and a wooden lookout platform on the right. There are two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and three [orichalcum ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ingot") immediately outside the entrance in an open-sided shelter.

### Mor Khazgur Mine

Mine interior

The entrance leads into a passage descending to the north, that leads into a large chamber with wooden scaffolding along the north and east walls and wooden planking shoring up the other two walls. Directly in front of the scaffolding is a long wooden table holding two orichalcum ingots, a piece of [orichalcum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") (which is free to take if you are [blood-kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the Orcs), and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). There are many pickaxes and several empty carts found in the mine. To the left of the table is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Climbing the ramp to the left to the first level leads to two orichlcum ore veins on the left. There is a basket containing a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") beside the first of these. Between the two veins is a passage heading down to the north, with two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") at the top, on the left. At the bottom are two more ore veins. Returning to the first ledge, along the front edge of the ledge are a couple of stacks of crates, barrels, two of sacks of foodstuffs, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") leaning against one crate and a loose piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") beside another.

In the main chamber there is a second ramp leading up from the first ledge heading east to a higher level. There is an ore vein on your left on the wall with a bedroll underneath it, a second ore vein on the wall to the east with a small wooden table in front, holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, and some bread and cheese. For the final ore vein; from the ground floor of the mine, there is a short tunnel to the west with an ore vein at the end.

Mor Khazgur

**Mor Khazgur** is an [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the far northwest of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

The stronghold contains three zones: *[Larak's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse")*, *[Mor Khazgur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Cellar "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Cellar")*, and *[Mor Khazgur Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Mine "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Mine")*.

The stronghold owns and operates an [orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum "Skyrim:Orichalcum") mine containing seven [ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein"). Notable NPCs found here include [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak"), a master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill, and [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart"), a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and potential [Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

As with all Orc Strongholds, you must become [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") to the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") before you are welcome in the stronghold and able to barter or receive other services.

([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

There is just a single entrance to the stronghold's compound near the northern edge of the surrounding palisade. There is a small vegetable patch immediately on your right upon entering, which contains eleven [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), eleven [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and eight [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. On the left is a lookout tower, while in front is a tree stump that has a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus growing from it. Behind the vegetables is an open-sided hut, beneath which is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a rack hanging from the ceiling holding a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid and [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

The path leads past the [longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse"), passing a wooden table and chair on the right where [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak") is generally found sitting. Beside this is a rack holding three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). On the other side of the entrance to the longhouse is a practice dummy where [Borgakh the Steel Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgakh_the_Steel_Heart "Skyrim:Borgakh the Steel Heart") is normally found training her skill-at-arms. Opposite the longhouse entrance is a second open-sided hut with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") beside it and a set of shelves under it. These hold an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), two random [potions of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and a sample of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi, two [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower").

Continuing past the longhouse there is a covered stack of food barrels on the right with a trapdoor leading to [Mor Khazgur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Cellar "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Cellar") beside them. On the left is a second lookout tower, while ahead is a covered blacksmithing area consisting of a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), with a set of shelves at the rear holding a random enchanted [Orcish battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Orcish Battleaxe"), a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")*, three owned [orichalcum ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ingot"), a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), an enchanted [Orcish sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Sword "Skyrim:Orcish Sword") and an [Orcish helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Helmet "Skyrim:Orcish Helmet") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Shield "Skyrim:Orcish Shield").

The path continues up and around, passing a second tree stump with mora tapinella fungus growing on it. Further up it passes between another lookout tower and a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") to the top where [Mor Khazgur Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Mine "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Mine") is located. On the right of the entrance are some more food barrels and three non-respawning orichalcum ingots.

| Crops | Mushrooms |
| --- | --- |
| 11 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  11 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  8 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 2 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") |

## Notes

- In the DialogueViews files for the game, there exists a line (likely meant for the gate guard) that was meant to quickly establish the stronghold: *"This is Mor Khazgur and we live under chief Larak. The rest is our business."*
- Mor Khazgur also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [a mine](/wiki/Online:Mor_Khazgur "Online:Mor Khazgur") and an [instanced Battleground](/wiki/Online:Mor_Khazgur_(battleground) "Online:Mor Khazgur (battleground)").

# Skyrim:More Than You Can Chew

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Obtain the secrets of crafting with [netch leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather") from a tribe of [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading *[Peddler's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Peddler%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Peddler's Journal")* |
| Location(s): | [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") |
| Reward: | Painted Netch Leather Armor, Netch Leather Armor, [Boots of Blinding Speed](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_of_Blinding_Speed "Skyrim:Boots of Blinding Speed"), ability to craft new armor pieces |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE041\_Quest, ccBGSSSE041\_MiscQuest |
| Added by: | [Netch Leather Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor") |

A tribe of hungry rieklings needs your help

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find the body of a Dark Elf north of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") and read the *[Peddler's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Peddler%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Peddler's Journal")*.
2. Speak with the [Riekling Tribe Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Tribe_Leader "Skyrim:Riekling Tribe Leader") on an island further north of the camp.
3. *(Optional)* Craft [Imitation Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Imitation Netch Leather").
4. Locate the [Giant Bull Netch](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Giant_Bull_Netch&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Giant Bull Netch (page does not exist)") and kill him *or* defend him from the rieklings.
5. Give either [Giant Bull Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Bull_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Giant Bull Netch Leather") or Imitation Netch Leather to the Riekling Tribe Leader for your reward.
6. *(Optional)* Read *[Crafting with Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Crafting_with_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Crafting with Netch Leather")* and craft a set of Netch Leather Armor *or* travel to [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") and search for a chest containing the [Boots of Blinding Speed](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_of_Blinding_Speed "Skyrim:Boots of Blinding Speed").

### Hungry Rieklings

Travel to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), to a small unmarked camp along the coast north of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"), not to be confused with the nearby camp of [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal") on an islet to the northwest.

At the camp, you will find the body of a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)") peddler who was apparently killed by [Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"). To start the quest, loot his body for the *[Peddler's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Peddler%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Peddler's Journal")*, which describes his interactions with a tribe of [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") from an island to the north. The peddler was attempting to trade with the rieklings, who had mistaken his netch leather armor for food. They also made off with a book explaining how to craft netch leather armor, believing it to be a cookbook. [Netch leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather") is of course highly toxic, which forced the peddler to begin importing regular leather from the mainland and dyeing it to fool the rieklings and prevent their untimely deaths.

After reading the book, you will need to swim northward to the riekling camp to meet with the [Riekling Tribe Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Tribe_Leader "Skyrim:Riekling Tribe Leader"). Unlike most of their kind, the rieklings on this island are non-hostile and will allow you to approach.

### Leather Delivery

Straight from the source

Riekling hunting party sketch

The Tribe Leader is a riekling of few words. After a brief one-sided exchange, he will hand you a [Riekling Hunting Party Sketch](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hunting_Party_Sketch "Skyrim:Riekling Hunting Party Sketch"), a crude drawing which identifies the location of a hunting party sent to track down a [Giant Bull Netch](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Giant_Bull_Netch&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Giant Bull Netch (page does not exist)"). At this point you will have several branching options for how to deal with the tribe.

You can attempt to pass a Very Hard [Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") check to convince the Tribe Leader that ingesting netch leather will kill him and that he should give you the crafting book. If you can't manage to convince him, your only option if you wish to save the rieklings is to use a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") to create [Imitation Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Imitation_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Imitation Netch Leather"), by combining regular [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") with [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). This can then be given to the Tribe Leader to progress the quest.

Alternatively, you can track down the hunting party along the coast just east of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone"). You will arrive to find a party of rieklings engaged in battle with a family of netches (the Giant Bull Netch along with a [Giant Betty Netch](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Giant_Betty_Netch&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Giant Betty Netch (page does not exist)") and a [Netch Calf](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Calf "Skyrim:Netch Calf")). Both sides are [protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs") so it will be up to you to deliver the killing blows and decide the battle. You can kill the rieklings in order to save the netch, or you can join in and claim the [Giant Bull Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Bull_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Giant Bull Netch Leather") for yourself. You can then deliver the leather to the Tribe Leader to progress the quest.

It is possible to obtain both the Giant Bull Netch Leather and the Imitation Netch Leather and decide which you want to give to the tribe. You can also just attack the Rieklings and loot the Tribe Leader's corpse.

Whichever choice you make, you will be rewarded with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Riekling_Chest "Skyrim:Key to Riekling Chest") which unlocks a nearby chest containing the book *[Crafting with Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Crafting_with_Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Crafting with Netch Leather")* as well as a full set of Painted Netch Leather armor. Loot the contents to complete the quest.

### Crafting with Netch Leather

The optional chest in Fort Hraggstad

Although the quest completes once you loot the chest, you will be given a [miscellaneous objective](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") to read the crafting book. Doing so will give you two further objectives: the option to either craft your own set of Netch Leather armor, or to instead track down a shipment somewhere in [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad").

It is advisable to search Fort Hraggstad for a full set rather than crafting your own, as the chest is located just inside the fort's main entrance and contains an additional unique item, the [Boots of Blinding Speed](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_of_Blinding_Speed "Skyrim:Boots of Blinding Speed"). This artifact is legendary for the extreme speed at which it allows the wearer to travel, although unfortunately it curses you with total blindness while equipped. This can be somewhat negated through the use of [Night Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(effect) "Skyrim:Night Eye (effect)"). Once you've obtained a set of Netch Leather armor, both objectives will complete.

## Notes

- The Boots of Blinding Speed previously appeared in [*TES III: Morrowind*](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind") and bore a similar enchantment which could likewise be negated through magical effects.
- The Painted Netch Leather Armor cannot be crafted and can only be found within the Riekling Tribe Chest. Its armor rating is higher than all the other variants.

## Bugs

- There is a charcoal *chunk* in a bucket near the forge at the Skaal Village, but you will not be able to craft the Imitation Netch Leather with it. You need to use a charcoal *stick* instead.

-  Rieklings are hostile from the start of the quest. Could be due to having a conjured or goblin follower. **?**

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE041_Quest, ccBGSSSE041_MiscQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE041_Quest, ccBGSSSE041_MiscQuest`.

# Skyrim:Morthal

## Overview

Morthal

**Morthal** is a city in the north of Skyrim, and the capital of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). It is initially aligned with the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), but [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") seems uninterested in the conflict, claiming to sense bigger things afoot in the world. Her reclusive nature and mysticism has fed a general perception that she is an ineffective ruler. Many residents are concerned about the war, which brings unwelcome outsiders, and would prefer to continue to live in isolation. The city itself is a fairly small, humble settlement of little economic or strategic importance besides its small lumber mill. Only the mill, an [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut"), and an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") support its weak economy. Sitting on the southern edge of the Drajkmyr marsh, Morthal is often shrouded in a thick fog. The ominous twisted trees and torches glowing in the fog like wisps present a foreboding appearance to travelers. The swampy surrounding lands are rich in [deathbells](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), and [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"). Leveled creatures ([trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") and rarely [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") in open space) spawn in the area at night.

For more information on Morthal, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Morthal "Lore:Morthal").

#### Side Quests

- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.
- **[Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn")**: Track down [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") to rid yourself of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

| [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") | **[Thane of Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Return to Sorli | [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)") or [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") |

#### Daedric

- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk")**: Silence a [terrible bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk"), permanently.

## Notes

- With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, you can purchase [a plot of land](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor") in Hjaalmarch to build a house on. Also, two [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") will be present.
- It's possible that Hroggar's house once had an interior cell, or was at least intended to have one. Unused location data for a "Burned House" with the editor ID of `MorthalBurnedHouseLocation` exists, but no other corroborating leftovers.
- Just outside town to the southeast is a Nordic barrow guarded by a leveled [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Inside, a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")* rests atop a shelf. To the left, the body of a novice [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") with a dagger in his chest can be found in front of an open tomb, next to a table with a [Scroll of Turn Lesser Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Turn_Lesser_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Turn Lesser Undead") on top of it, and a [Staff of Revenants](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Revenants#Staff_of_Revenants "Skyrim:Staff of Revenants"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-29832&y=60737&zoom=8&legacy=true)
- Also outside town to the northwest, another Nordic barrow contains a novice-locked chest with a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Locked Room](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Locked_Room "Skyrim:The Locked Room")* beside it. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-48095&y=76564&zoom=8&legacy=true)
- Despite going unnamed in the final game as it has no interiors or map markers, the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* refers to the local mill as **Marshdeep Camp**.
- Music doesn't play outdoors when you're here, except during special events like dragon fights.
- Morthal also [appears](/wiki/Online:Morthal "Online:Morthal") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The water wheel at the mill rotates clockwise, but turns the wrong way given the direction of the water current.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Mortrag Peak

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Mortrag Peak ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mortrag+Peak)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Mortrag_Peak "Lore:Mortrag Peak")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Wilderness 8, 20 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| North of [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow") South of [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins") | |

Mortrag Peak, as seen from the southeast

**Mortrag Peak** is one of the highest points on Solstheim, south of [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins"). The marker for this peak does not appear on the compass until you have [climbed](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") nearly to the top.

The ascent of this peak can be started from the entrance to [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow"). Jump up the low rocks behind the barrow entrance, and head in a northerly direction towards the highest point. There are some snow-covered tracks that make this section easier. A [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") ore vein lies beside the snowy track at the base of a sheer rock face; head around the rock to the right of this vein, and continue jumping higher. Reaching the cliff face marks the extent of the 'easy' section of this climb.

A narrow slope leads up the cliff face at 45 degrees to horizontal. When this gets too steep, you should notice a small ledge at the same level off to the right. By pushing forward into the face of the mountain at the same time as moving to the right, you can reach this ledge. The aim from here is to get to the saddle-shaped ridge roughly four character-heights above your head. This can be done by moving around to the other side of the promontory you are standing on the western side of, as the slope on the eastern side is shallower. You can then zig-zag your way up the slope to the saddle.

Your next waypoint is the ledge partway up the left side of the peak. Jump towards and around it to reach a lower section on its western side. Continue up the ledge, then zig-zag up the slope to your left to reach the narrow ridge at the top. Jump along this ridge towards the peak.

You will need to carefully jump and edge your way around to the left to reach a better vantage point for gaining the summit. Note that the summit is poorly meshed and is unstable; you will not be able to find a place to stand without sliding downwards or into the mountain. The closest stable point is on the ridge just below the top; trigger the location marker, and retreat to this ridge to survey the scenery.

To the north lie the ruins of Castle Karstaag. To the east is [Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak"), with [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") just visible behind it. In the clearing to the southeast, the remains of [a stone memorial](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hrothmund%27s_Bane "Bloodmoon:Hrothmund's Bane") mark the entrance to [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow"). To the south, you can see [Mount Moesring](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Moesring "Skyrim:Mount Moesring") and the ruins of [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"). In the southwest, partially hidden by the peak of the mountain, a small burial chamber contains the [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source").

## Notes

- Using [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and riding him can make climbing the mountain easier.
-  The `tmm` command won't make it visible on the map.

# Skyrim:Morvayn Ancestral Tomb

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cemetery: Morvayn Ancestral Tomb ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Morvayn+Ancestral+Tomb)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRMorvaynTomb | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |

Morvayn Ancestral Tomb

The **Morvayn Ancestral Tomb** is a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") ancestral tomb in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is northwest of the flight of stairs leading up to the [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple"), opposite the entrance to [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor").

It is where members of the Morvayn family of [House Redoran](/wiki/Lore:House_Redoran "Lore:House Redoran") are interred if they die on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). Past members of the family include [Remas](/wiki/Morrowind:Remas_Morvayn "Morrowind:Remas Morvayn") and his wife [Brara Morvayn](/wiki/Morrowind:Mistress_Brara_Morvayn "Morrowind:Mistress Brara Morvayn"), House Redoran Councilors of Vvardenfell and the parents of [Lleril Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn"), the current Councilor of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") and the formal ruler of Solstheim, as well as [Varel Morvayn](/wiki/Oblivion:Varel_Morvayn "Oblivion:Varel Morvayn"), a smith resident in [Anvil](/wiki/Oblivion:Anvil "Oblivion:Anvil").

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is a [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plant and three food urns. To the right of the entrance are three more scathecraw plants, two more food urns, and a lit brazier. The entrance has an expert-level lock.

### Morvayn Ancestral Tomb

The entrance from outside leads into a corridor lined with four lit braziers which proceeds north to the tomb room. In the room, to the east is an alcove with a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Tomb_Key "Skyrim:Raven Rock Tomb Key")-locked door to the [Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb"). The key can be obtained as part of the quest [Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep"). The room features a total of four ash piles littered with bones, with the central pile surrounded by steps and lit candles. Also in the room are nine ash yam urns, two benches, ten unusable barrels, and four more lit braziers around the central pile.

# Skyrim:Morvayn Manor

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Morvayn Manor ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Morvayn+Manor)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRMorvaynManor, DLC2RRMorvaynManorChambers | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Morvayn Manor

**Morvayn Manor** is the home of [Lleril Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn"), [Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano"), and [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is on the waterfront between [Caerellius House](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House "Skyrim:Caerellius House") to the southeast and [Glover Mallory's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House") to the northwest, opposite the entrance to the [Morvayn Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Morvayn Ancestral Tomb").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano")  [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano")  [Lleril Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance are five [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants, a food urn, two unusable barrels, and an empty cart. To the right of the entrance is a [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root"), three more scathecraw plants, and five unusable barrels. Along the sides and back of the building on the waterfront are two ash yam urns, three unusable barrels, and three crates. A [Redoran guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") is posted outside the entrance, which is unlocked.

### Morvayn Manor

Morvayn Manor throne room

The entrance leads into the main room, where First Councilor [Lleril Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") holds court on his throne, protected by a Redoran guard posted next to the entrance. Along the west wall opposite the entrance are three chairs and a table holding a bottle each of [flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Flin "Skyrim:Flin"), [matze](/wiki/Skyrim:Matze "Skyrim:Matze"), [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), three bowls of [horker and ash yam stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_and_Ash_Yam_Stew "Skyrim:Horker and Ash Yam Stew"), two [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), and a piece of [cooked boar meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Boar_Meat "Skyrim:Cooked Boar Meat"). To the south of the table are two benches along the east and west walls. Along the curved south wall is a chair often occupied by Second Councilor [Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano"), the throne, and a sideboard holding a bottle each of matze, shein, and flin, a sample of [Felsaad tern feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern_Feathers "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern Feathers"), and copies of *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")*, *[Bone, Part II](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_II "Skyrim:Bone, Part II")*, and *[The True Noble's Code](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Noble%27s_Code "Skyrim:The True Noble's Code")*. The wall ledge holds the following items, starting from behind the throne along the south wall and ending at the doorway to the next room along the north wall: bottles of sujamma, matze, shein, sujamma, flin, and shein, copies of all three volumes of *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*, both volumes of *[The Red Year](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year "Skyrim:The Red Year")*, *[The Poison Song, Book I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_I "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book I")*, and *[The Poison Song, Book II](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_II "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book II")*, two bottles of wine, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of sujamma, and copies of *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")* and *[Words of the Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_of_the_Wind "Skyrim:Words of the Wind")*.

The next room is circular, and features the stairs leading up to the upper floor. Along the curved west wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), a wood pile, a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand over a fire, a braid of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a [dead rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack, and a food urn. Along the north wall beneath the stairs is a set of shelves holding three loaves of bread, a bottle each of wine, alto wine, matze, shein, and flin, two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), four ash yams, an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), an eidar cheese wedge, two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Above the set of shelves are two dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two dried [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and two garlic braids hanging from the ceiling, and to the right of the set of shelves is a sack, two food urns, an ingredient urn, an ash yam urn, and a crate.

The small circular room on the upper floor contains three food urns, an ash yam urn, a wood pile, three crates, one of which has a sample of Felsaad tern feathers on top, two sacks, an unusable barrel, and a straw bale. An adept-locked door on the south wall leads to the second zone, *Morvayn Manor Chambers*.

### Morvayn Manor Chambers

The entrance leads into Adril and [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano")'s bedroom. In the southwest corner is a set of shelves holding two bottles of wine, two bottles of shein, a bottle of matze, a copy of *The Poison Song, Book II*, a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), an ash yam, a sliced goat cheese, and two eidar cheese wheels. On the wall ledge near the set of shelves are three more bottles of alto wine, a bottle of shein, and a bottle of wine, and to the right of the set of shelves is a bucket containing three more ash yams. In the northwest corner is a chair and a small round table holding a piece of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), with a bottle each of shein and matze on the wall shelf above the table, and an unlocked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on the wall ledge to the right of the table. In the southeast corner is an owned double bed, with two bottles of shein, a bottle of flin, and a bottle of matze on the wall ledge to the right of the bed. In the northeast corner is a bench. Along the north wall is a door to the next room.

The next room is circular, and serves as Lleril Morvayn's bedroom. Along the west wall is an expert-locked display case containing a [chitin heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Chitin Heavy Armor") cuirass and a [chitin heavy helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Heavy_Helmet "Skyrim:Chitin Heavy Helmet"). Along the north wall is an owned double bed, with a sideboard at its foot holding copies of *History of Raven Rock, Vol. I* and *II*, two notes titled *[House Redoran's Reply](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Redoran%27s_Reply "Skyrim:House Redoran's Reply")* and *[Adril's Survey Results](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril%27s_Survey_Results "Skyrim:Adril's Survey Results")*, and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). Along the east wall is a chair and a set of shelves holding three bottles of flin, a bottle of matze, a bottle of sujamma, copies of *[The Five Far Stars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Five_Far_Stars "Skyrim:The Five Far Stars")* and *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*, a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"). Although it is possible to jump onto the rafters under the domed ceiling, there are no items on the rafters.

## Bugs

- There isn't enough bed space in Morvayn Manor for the Arano couple to be able to sleep in their assigned upstairs area.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.4, addresses this issue. Their bed has been upgraded to a double, and the navmesh has been adjusted to fit the new sleeping arrangements.
- The East Empire Company strongbox here is unlocked, rather than expert-locked like almost all other East Empire Company strongboxes.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Several buildings in Raven Rock, including Morvayn Manor, were incorrectly assigned the [music](/wiki/Skyrim:Music "Skyrim:Music") heard in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") rather than the default Solstheim music heard in other houses.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=11969))
- The music bug listed above also affects the Morvayn Manor Chambers.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17929))

# Skyrim:Morvunskar

## Overview

Morvunskar

**Morvunskar** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and their leader [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked"). It contains only one zone, *[Morvunskar](#Morvunskar)*.

The [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") realm [Misty Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Misty_Grove "Skyrim:Misty Grove") is accessed here during the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember").

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The fort's tactical position is evidenced by its view of Windhelm to the northeast and [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") to the southeast, and also by the large number of main roads visible from its towers. The entrance tunnel through the southern wall has a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") near the beginning that activates four different [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"), starting from the far end and moving toward the plate. Upstairs in a small courtyard are three bedrolls beneath wooden shelters around a campfire. The door to the interior of the fort is west of the fire, and there is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") by the bedroll to the north.

Five mages guard the exterior of the fort. The first can be seen in a wooden guard tower above the entrance tunnel, while two others patrol the first courtyard. The fourth patrols the stairs up to the camp, and the fifth is sitting in a chair by the fire. The warlocks have a high detection level, making a [stealthy approach](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") difficult, though the fort can be accessed from the western side due to landslides that have made the ground level with the height of the walls.

### Morvunskar

The forge

The kitchen

Looking across to the throne

Looking down to Naris the Wicked

The shrine of Dibella

There are unusually large numbers of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [empty wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") bottles in the fort.

If you go silently to your right after entering, you will overhear two mages having a conversation in a room to the northwest:

**Mage #1**: *"They drink all day and night and what do I do?"*
**Mage #2**: *"You work the forge."*
**Mage #1**: *"I work the forge."*
**Mage #1**: *"Why do they need me to do this? We use magic, not weapons. I swear they make me do this for a laugh. At least I'm not dealing with the prisoners down below."*
**Mage #2**: *"Yeah, I don't know how I feel about what goes on down there."*
**Mage #1**: *"I bet Naris gets a kick out it*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*. Nasty fella he is."*
**Mage #2**: *"You better quiet down before you end up there. Then I'd have to work the forge."*

The room the mages are in contains a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a bed, and a table holding three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Cherim's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Cherim%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Cherim's Heart")*. The door beside this room is barred from the other side. The room opposite the main entrance is the kitchen, and contains a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over a campfire, a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"); a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hang from several racks.

In the middle of the entrance room are two fire braziers that mark the onward path, which is down some steps and through an unlocked door. A [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") grows to the left of the stairs. Beyond the door is a narrow passage that turns twice before ending at another wooden door. Through the door is a wide passage, with a small wooden table on the left holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a bottle of wine, and six loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins. Opposite the table is a small end table holding a small mead barrel.

At the end of the passage are stairs leading down into a large chamber with several hostile mages. To the left before a pile of rubble ahead to the north is a pressure plate that activates flame spout traps from the left wall. The chamber is in two sections, with several pillars throughout. A wide flight of double stairs on the right leads up to the boss mage and another mage. There are four [troll skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") between the double flight of stairs, and at the top two chairs on raised sections with more stairs leading up to them act as improvised thrones. Beside the higher of the two chairs is a small end table, and to the left is an unlocked chest. (Note: A portal to Misty Grove appears to the right of the thrones if you are on the quest A Night To Remember. The area affected by the portal to Misty Grove is larger than its physical appearance, and may extend even to the small storeroom below the throne area. If the portal is active, you will therefore need to hug the left wall and proceed slowly toward the end table and chest to avoid being transported.) Near the bottom of the double stairs is a toppled set of shelves leaning against the side of the stairs by a pillar; the shelves hold many empty wine bottles and bottles of wine.

The left side of the chamber has several small tables and chairs, quite a few of which have been overturned. Another mage patrols this area. Against the west wall is a set of shelves holding six common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack. To the north is an opening leading into another passage, with a doorway under the stairs nearby to the east leading into a small storeroom containing a novice-locked chest, an adept-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), and two food barrels. The passage to the north has a pressure plate that triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") from the right. Just after this trap is a T-junction, with passages leading to the right and straight ahead. Ahead are two bedrooms. The bedroom on the left contains a long wooden table against the south wall with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") built in, an unowned double bed against the north wall with an end table to the right, and a set of shelves to the left holding twelve common books and a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). The bedroom on the right contains two unowned single beds and a small square wooden table. Taking the passage to the right brings you past several stacks of unusable barrels; around the corner, a mage is sitting at a table on the left. Beside the table is a sideboard holding four more common books, and a second table and chairs.

The passage then turns to the west, with a novice-locked door on the east wall and another room ahead containing three unowned bedrolls, a [shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrines"), two end tables, and a round wooden table holding two bottles of alto wine. The end tables hold two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a leveled potion of invisibility, respectively. Through the novice-locked door is a flight of stairs leading down to Naris the Wicked and the results of his "experiments". You may even overhear some of his comments about his experiments, such as the *"...sweet smell of burnt flesh."* He is standing in front of a wooden gated cell, with six [burnt corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Containers") among some burning coals inside. The lever to open the gate is on the wall to the left. Also to the left is an unlocked chest, and to the right is a set of shelves and a round wooden table holding a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v3 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v3")* and a leveled poison.

The passage turns to the west, passing a table covered in blood holding a small coin purse and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Opposite the table is a set of shelves holding eight common books. From here the passage climbs and turns south. At the top is the barred door, providing a shortcut to the exit.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is west of the path up to the fort.
- A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are west of the fort. To reach them, go west around the rocks from the bottom of the path to the fort, then head north until directly west of the Morvunskar map marker.
- A [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") is at the end of a short path east of the main road toward Windhelm, with an assortment of weapons and items at its base.
- 105 empty wine bottles are scattered throughout the fort.
- Morvunskar also [appears](/wiki/Online:Fort_Morvunskar "Online:Fort Morvunskar") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") can sometimes be found in Morvunskar fighting the mages in the large room downstairs. This can happen at any time after the quest A Night To Remember has started. Sanguine is not leveled, but is [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs"), so the fight can go on endlessly. If Morvunskar is the target of a [*Dawnguard* quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"), the master vampire may join the fight with Sanguine and the mages. If this bug has occurred, you will probably hear the battle in progress shortly after you enter the interior. If you are in werewolf form, Sanguine may attack you as well; running away solves this.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- If you return to Morvunskar after completing A Night To Remember, sometimes the portal to Misty Grove will still be accessible. Passing through it will end with you being stuck in Misty Grove, as Sanguine is no longer there to teleport you out.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - Reload a save from before you entered.
  -  On the PC, you can open the console and type `tcl` to toggle collision, then fly under the map just below where you enter Misty Grove to find a door that will take you back to Morvunskar.
- In the large central room where the portal to Misty Grove appears, you may encounter up to seven assorted magic casters. Depending on circumstances, if they all attack, their spell-related graphics (lightning, fire blasts, etc.) may cause the game to crash or lock up. Making a save before entering the room is advisable. **?**
- If you're sent here by [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar") to kill a [Volkihar Master Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Master_Vampire "Skyrim:Volkihar Master Vampire") for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"), sneak through to the vampire and do that first or he may fall through the floor, making it impossible to complete the quest. **?**

# Skyrim:Morwen's House

## Overview

|  |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2SVMorwensHouse | |
| Region | |

| [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") | |

Morwen's House

**Morwen's House** is the home of [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the north side of the village, between [Edla's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla%27s_House "Skyrim:Edla's House") to the west and the [Greathall](/wiki/Skyrim:Greathall "Skyrim:Greathall") to the southeast. The player can choose to move into the home if they have [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") Morwen.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen") |

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is a bench. Along the west wall are two fish barrels and an archery target. Behind the house is a sparring dummy and a wood pile. Along the east wall is a bench often occupied by [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)"), a crate with a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") on top, and a fish barrel. The entrance has a novice lock.

### Morwen's House

The entrance leads into a two-room home. There is a small area on your left with a dresser against the east wall. On the dresser is a [steel horned helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Horned_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Horned Helmet"), a pair of [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), and a wooden plate with a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace") on top of it. To the right in the southeast corner is a chair. There is an open crate with a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") resting in it and a basket with a quiver of [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") to the right. There is a shield plaque with a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") and two crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") on the west wall of this small area.

House-proud

To the right of the door against the east wall is a set of shelves containing [Banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor"), a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), a [steel plate helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Plate Helmet"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"). to the left against the north wall is a narrow table with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"). To the left of this still against the north wall are two shelves, on the shelves is a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a bottle of ale, copies of *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_Prince "Skyrim:Beggar Prince")* and *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")*, a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") and two sacks. Beside the shelves, on the left is a chair, a barrel with a mead barrel on top and a cupboard with three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a wooden bowl containing an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") on the shelves. On a ledge against the west wall are three sacks.

Very house-proud

In the center of the room is a fire pit with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a cast iron pot containing a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and two [clam meats](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") around it. and hanging above in front of the door are a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") sample. There is a low railing between the door and the fire pit. Between the fire pit and the west wall is an open crate containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and two fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"). three small steps lead to the southern part of the house.

Table for one

There is a long table against the southern wall that separates the bedroom from the rest of the house. On the table is a mead barrel, three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a green apple and a plate containing a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). There is a shelf on the west wall above the table with a bottle of wine on it. and hanging above the table is a rack with two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and a rabbit. To the left of the table, on the floor is a bucket containing five bottles of ale. To the right of the fire pit against the east wall is a row of three weapon racks with a [Nordic bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Bow "Skyrim:Nordic Bow") and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). A sack is to the right of it and a bucket containing a quiver of [Nordic arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Arrow "Skyrim:Nordic Arrow") is to the left.

There is a doorway to the left of the table that leads to a small bedroom. On your left as you enter is an adept-locked display case containing a [glass war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_War_Axe "Skyrim:Glass War Axe"). There is a shelf underneath with a mead barrel and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). To the right are two barrels, a sack a in the corner a practice dummy. Half way along the south wall is an open crate with nine [iron daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), with three more on the floor next to it. In the southwestern corner is a chair. opposite against the wall that separates the bedroom from the rest of the house is a single bed with a shelf above it containing a copy of *[Troll Slaying](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Slaying "Skyrim:Troll Slaying")*. Finally at the end of the bed is a chest.

# Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| **Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.** | |

| Suggested Level: | 8 see [bugs](#Bugs) |

.jpg)

Injured Valdr waiting for help outside the cavern

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern").
2. Speak to [Valdr](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") directly outside of it.
3. Give Valdr anything he can use to help heal himself or heal him yourself.
4. Help Valdr clear the [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") out of Moss Mother Cavern, or do it alone.

### Spriggan Ambush

The first time you approach [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern"), [Valdr](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") will call out for your attention. He explains that he was attacked by [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") living in the cave and needs immediate medical attention or he'll die from the spriggan's curse. After helping him, he will further explain that his companions had tracked an injured [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") sow to the cave and were ambushed by the spriggans as they entered to kill it. Valdr was the only one to escape as [Ari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ari "Skyrim:Ari") and [Niels](/wiki/Skyrim:Niels "Skyrim:Niels") were killed before they could flee. He'll ask for your help to avenge his friends by killing the creatures.

### Vengeance

Valdr will offer to help you clear the caves. He uses a bow and becomes [protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs") if he follows you inside the cave. If you don't want to risk him dying, you can offer to clear the cave alone. There are three leveled spriggans and a single leveled bear. The bear and a spriggan will be near the entrance; the other two spriggans are near the pool. It's possible to engage them individually; any sort of [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") helps tremendously, though you may need to bring potions to mitigate their high damage output and ability to fully heal themselves. When all the spriggans are dead, Valdr will thank you and give you his [lucky dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr%27s_Lucky_Dagger "Skyrim:Valdr's Lucky Dagger") which has a 25% chance to critically hit. He states he will return to [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") after he finishes burying his friends. Search the cave for a few scattered pieces of loot, including leveled boots, shield and a one-handed weapon. See [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern") for more details.

## Notes

- If you are level 16 or above, you can ask the innkeeper at [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") about rumors and start the quest from [stage 5](#Quest_Stages).
- Valdr is not a protected NPC unless he becomes a follower during the quest so he may already be dead when you find Moss Mother Cavern. In that event, you will not be able to start the quest, even from the innkeeper.
- If you delay healing Valdr for any reason, he may die.
- If you head back to the road or wander off with him as a companion he'll stop following you and will return toward cavern saying in scripted comment:*"Changed your mind? Well, I can't give up so easily. I'm heading back"*. Then leaves the script adding: *"All right, then."*, *"Hmm hmm."* or *"Until next time."* But if you return too when approaching iron ore vein along the path he will rush toward you and start to follow again. Wandering off and returning again with him as a companion will produce the same action, though without scripted or any other comments now. One way or another, quest objective stays the same in your diary.
- It might be advisable to accept Valdr's help if you are doing this quest at a low level, as spriggans and bears are some of the toughest enemies for low-level players.
- Valdr's Lucky Dagger is one of the better weapons in the game at low levels, particularly for assassin-type characters who value burst damage. However, it is outclassed at higher levels by items such as the [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe").
- With version 2.0.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), Valdr will no longer trigger his script to keep him damaged when the quest has not started. Furthermore, he will now no longer heal himself before you have a chance to do so.

## Bugs

- Valdr may not accept anything besides a standard healing potion. Additionally, it may be impossible to interact with him in order to give him a potion.
  - Healing him with [Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Healing Hands") spell may bypass this bug.
- At higher levels, Valdr may actually have enough health to be considered healed as soon as you meet him, and he will thank you for your help.
- Valdr should return to [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") upon completion, but sometimes disappears.
- The quest may sometimes be finished, but stay in your journal at the "Locate Valdr's hunting party" stage. The reward is given regardless.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
  - A fix for the PC version is to type in the console `setstage dunMossMotherQST 10` followed by `setstage dunMossMotherQST 20`
- If you let Valdr initiate the conversation then talk to him before he finishes, but after you have received his lucky dagger, you'll receive a second one. **?**
- If you choose to clear the cavern without his assistance, he may be hostile when you return to him.
- When attempting to view this quest on the map, it will incorrectly focus on the north section of the map.
- Valdr may not talk to you.
  - Entering Moss Mother Cavern and exiting again usually fixes this.
  - Typing `setstage dunMossMotherQST 30` into the console should fix this.
  - Should Valdr not be outside the Cavern and none of the above work, go to the Cavern and use the following console commands to move Valdr to your location: `prid 411B9`  to select Valdr, `moveto player` to move him to your location.

## Quest Stages

| Moss Mother Cavern (dunMossMotherQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | *Objective 5:* Locate Valdr's hunting party. |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Heal Valdr's injuries. |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Clear out Moss Mother Cavern. |
| 40 |  | *Objective 30:* Clear out Moss Mother Cavern. |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Return to Valdr. *(if you told Valdr to wait)* |
| 105 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 9, 15, 20, 45, 60, 100, 101.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunMossMotherQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunMossMotherQST`.

# Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern

## Overview

This article is about the place. For the quest, see [Moss Mother Cavern (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)").

Moss Mother Cavern

**Moss Mother Cavern** is a small, open-roofed [cavernous](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") grove lush with many kinds of flora and fungi, located due north of [Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest") and northwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") which is inhabited by bears and spriggans.

You may be directed here by asking the [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Valga_Vinicia "Skyrim:Valga Vinicia") at [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") about rumors once you are level 16. She will inform you of a missing hunting party, which will initiate the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)") to locate them.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)")**: Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.

### Exterior

As you approach the cave for the first time, [Valdr](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr"), a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer"), beckons you to help him: *"Hello? You! Over here! Please, I need help!"* His hunting party chased a wounded [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") sow into the cave, and was ambushed by [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). His companions [Ari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ari "Skyrim:Ari") and [Niels](/wiki/Skyrim:Niels "Skyrim:Niels") were not so lucky, and can be found dead inside. Valdr requires immediate healing, or he will die due to his injuries: *"I may have lost a drop or two of blood. Truth is, I'm not going anywhere like this. Hurts to breathe."* There are many plants and fungi near the entrance, of the same types as found inside.

After the quest is complete and some time has passed in game, two graves will appear outside, in front of the log where Valdr is first found.

### Moss Mother Cavern

Moss Mother Cavern interior

As its name suggests, there is a lot of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") that can be harvested from the various ledges throughout the cave system. It is also a good spot to harvest [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungi. Other flora and fungi present inside the cave include various colors of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot").

The cave consists of two main areas linked by a sunken path; the second chamber contains a small interior pool. Opposite the entrance, on a ledge by a rock pillar is a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), with a leveled [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") close by. Ari's corpse is lying in front of the hunted dead bear, next to two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). The path continues to the east, passing beneath a fallen tree that spans between the ledges. A hollow tree stump in a corner to the northwest along this path contains some leveled loot, including a coin purse, potion, and weapon.

On the left ledge behind the pillar is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Using the fallen tree to cross to the right ledge and heading back toward the exit takes you to an adept-locked chest with an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in front of it.

As you continue along the path, look for a coin purse in the foliage on the ground to your right. There is another fallen tree on the left, with Niels' corpse in front, to the left of the pool. A nearby tree hides a second spriggan. To the east, near the rear of the second chamber, you'll find the last of the spriggans. There are more bear traps in this second chamber in deep undergrowth. Along a path northeast of the pool, near a towering tree, look around to find a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"). At the end of the cave, on a ledge by the southern wall, a boss chest can be found, along with a random [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), a potion, and a pair of boots. A random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons") can be found lying at the bottom of the pool near a skeleton.

# Skyrim:Mossy Glen Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Mossy Glen Cave | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"), [Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1HunterValleyCave01 | |

Mossy Glen Cave

**Mossy Glen Cave** is a small, unmarked bear den only accessible via [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon").

It is a natural cave with several stone pillars and plant matter throughout the cave.

## Exterior

There are two entrances, the first of which is found by heading uphill on a path to the north, past the point along the main path where you first see [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") upon entry to the canyon. There is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush outside this entrance, among the rocks to the left. To find the second entrance, head north from the entrance of Fort Dawnguard. When the path reaches its first switchback, continue due north, and you will pass between wooden palisade wall sections; the cave entrance is in the northern corner behind some trees. There are two snowberry bushes by this entrance.

## Mossy Glen Cave

The cave is dense with vegetation. Entering via the first entrance leads into an area with a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). On the second ledge along the wall to your left, there are two unlocked chests with minor loot. In the northernmost room, there are four leveled [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). After defeating the bears, check the west side of the room for another unlocked chest containing minor loot. On the east side of the cave, a narrow tunnel leads from the second entrance. There is another narrow tunnel directly opposite, which leads to the open area by the skeever. A [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and four [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungi can be found inside the cave.

## Bugs

- Navmesh in Mossy Glen Cave has several issues with triangles going up walls, broken links, and a complete lack of cover data.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Mossy Glen Cave interior

# Skyrim:Mount Anthor

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dragon Lair.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dragon_Lair.png) | Dragon Lair: Mount Anthor ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mount+Anthor)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Mount_Anthor "Lore:Mount Anthor")) | | |
