Mount Anthor

**Mount Anthor** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the word wall will be guarded by two leveled [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock").

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, there is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") on the altar in the middle of the lair, one urn, and one burial urn. At the top of the main stairway in the center of the lair is the word wall.

## Notes

- Mount Anthor is the only dragon lair with no treasure chest.
- The path southwest up the mountain to the lair continues to the south, then east, looping back to the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"). It appears that an avalanche killed a party of [refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugee "Skyrim:Refugee") on this path. Their three bodies, along with a wrecked cart piled up with their belongings, can be found partially buried in the snow. Among the detritus are a few useful items: a coin purse, a potion, an apothecary's satchel, a leveled battleaxe, and a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Enchanter's Primer](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Primer "Skyrim:Enchanter's Primer")*.
- Mount Anthor was the site of the battle between [Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Lore:Olaf_One-Eye "Lore:Olaf One-Eye") and the dragon Numinex which occurred during the [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era").
- Mount Anthor also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Mount_Anthor "Legends:Mount Anthor") in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends").

## Bugs

- If the dragon at the wall is the subject of a bounty, it may not appear after the main quest has been completed.
- Sometimes after killing the dragon, you won't absorb its soul. You may also be unable to harvest Dragon Heartscales with [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Kahvozein.27s_Fang "Skyrim:Quest Items").
- If the dragon is killed while on the stairs, occasionally the skeletal remains will clip incorrectly and fall through the stairs, rendering the dragon soul unavailable. **?**
- The dragon sometimes doesn't spawn correctly. This sometimes causes the compass to point toward an incorrect location, even if the map itself centers on the correct location.
  -  If the dragon is the target of a quest, you may use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `sqt` to review the quest variables for the dragon's [reference ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID"), then use further commands to force the dragon to appear or respawn. For example, if the dragon's reference ID is "32AC2", the command `prid 32AC2` followed by the command `moveto player` should force the dragon to appear. Alternatively, if the dragon isn't dead or disabled (i.e., `prid 32AC2` then `getdead` and `getdisabled` both return "0"), you can instead use `prid 32AC2` followed by `resetai`, which should cause the dragon to start circling the area again after a few seconds. Finally, you may simply skip the quest by using the command `setstage quest ID 100` (see the relevant quest page to confirm the quest ID and stage variables).
  - You may use splash damage spells (Fireball, runes, etc.) to damage the dragon hiding in the terrain. Cast the spell in the direction of the arrow icon on the map, and the dragon should reappear.

# Skyrim:Mount Moesring

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Mount Moesring ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Mount+Moesring)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Wilderness 10, 15 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag") South of [Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass") | |

Mount Moesring, seen from the south

**Mount Moesring** is one of the highest points on Solstheim, south of [Moesring Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Moesring_Pass "Skyrim:Moesring Pass"). The marker for this peak does not appear on the compass until you have [climbed](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") nearly to the top.

On foot, it is best to start your climb just north of the [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar"). Once you reach a lower peak, it's advisable to save, as falls from this height can kill you. Leap across the gap from the lower peak, keeping as much height as possible, then continue climbing while circling clockwise around the peak to reach the top, where you can stand without slipping. See [this article](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") for tips on mountain climbing.

From the top, you can see most of Solstheim, even at night. To the immediate north is Moesring Pass with [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow") beyond, and both [Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak") and [Frykte Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frykte_Peak "Skyrim:Frykte Peak") etched against the sky in the distance. To the west you can see [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"), while to the southwest is [Hvitkald Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hvitkald_Peak "Skyrim:Hvitkald Peak"), with [the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark") protecting Raven Rock clearly visible to the left of the peak. Far to the south is the [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall"), with the circular path leading up to [Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove") carved into the landscape. To the south-southeast is [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower"), and farther to the southeast is the settlement of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"), with the Red Mountain belching ash and rock into the sky beyond. To the east is the massive stonework surrounding the [Tree Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Tree_Stone "Skyrim:Tree Stone") at the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"). The view between the Temple of Miraak to the east and Moesring Pass to the north is blocked by another mountain range.

## Notes

- Using [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and riding him can make climbing the mountain easier.
-  The `tmm` command won't make it visible on the map.

# Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") |
| Location(s): | [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold and [Muiri's Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Muiri's Ring") (if optional task is completed), otherwise 100 gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") if optional task is completed) |
| ID: | DB03 |
| Suggested Level: | 12 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), or [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | **Next →** [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"), [Kill Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Beitild "Skyrim:Kill Beitild"), or [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius") | | → Next | [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") | | |

[Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") pulls the strings

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri").
2. *(Optional)* Kill [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield").
3. Travel to [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and kill [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont").
4. Return to Muiri for your reward.

### Let the Mourning Begin

After completing at least one of [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir")'s contracts, returning to the [Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") will trigger a scene where a seemingly annoyed [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") reluctantly welcomes [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") to the hideout. As Nazir will deny you any rewards before you speak to Astrid, let the conversation finish and then wait for her to approach you. She will hand you the first real job for the Brotherhood: [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") resident [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") wants an ex-lover killed. Astrid asks you to show professionalism and explains that you can keep the entire reward, as this is your first contract.

In Markarth, Muiri will be at work in [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") during the day and hanging out in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") in the evening. Approach her and witness her surprise that the Dark Brotherhood actually still exists and that the [Sacrament](/wiki/Lore:Black_Sacrament "Lore:Black Sacrament") worked. She then explains the story of how she was once a very close friend of the [Shatter-Shield family](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") until she met womanizer [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont"). Alain managed to seduce her but, as it turned out, used her to get close to the Shatter-Shield family and rob them blind. The love affair ended with Muiri being kicked out in the cold by the family and Dufont abandoning her, eventually rejoining his bandit colleagues inside [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar").

Muiri understandably wants Alain dead, but will make a second request once you arrive, promising to raise the reward if carried out. Muiri wants [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield") assassinated as well, as an act of revenge on the family. Recently the Shatter-Shield family lost youngest daughter Friga to a [serial killer](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") and their mourning process was part of Dufont's plan and the very reason he seduced Muiri. The family held Muiri responsible and refused to talk to her ever again. Muiri now reasons they may see just how wrong it was to kick her out if their only remaining daughter dies. You automatically accept the task, but it is optional. Asking her for elaboration will net you two samples of poisonous [lotus extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Lotus_Extract "Skyrim:Lotus Extract"), which may come in handy.

### Nilsine

:   *Note: If you have yet to trigger the quest [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"), do so before killing Nilsine Shatter-Shield. See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice#How_to_Start_the_Quest "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") for details. If there is a dead woman lying near the Windhelm Hall of the Dead, then Blood on the Ice has been triggered.*

Windhelm's citizens know of the tragedy that recently hit the wealthy Shatter-Shield family and will often talk about the serial killer's first victim, Friga Shatter-Shield. When speaking to the grieving parents, [Tova](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") and [Torbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield"), both will express great sadness, especially Tova. Unaware that Muiri plans her revenge, the family, including your target Nilsine Shatter-Shield, tries to move on in life. Nilsine roams around town all day long: browsing the market in the morning, standing near her sister's now-abandoned house, [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), in the afternoon, and spending her evenings inside the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)") on weekdays and in the [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos") on weekends. It is not possible to trigger her anger during conversation, so a stealthy kill when she is alone in the evening is preferable. When the deed is done, move on to the real target, [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont"), or return to Muiri in Markarth. Killing Nilsine will cause her already bereaved mother, Tova, to commit suicide in their clan home in Windhelm.

### Raldbthar

[Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont") and one of his guards

Raldbthar is a Dwemer ruin located on the snowy mountainside east of [Korvanjund](/wiki/Skyrim:Korvanjund "Skyrim:Korvanjund"), past [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint"). It is one of the three entrances to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). The target, however, has taken up residence in the first zone, so the trek will not be long. A few bandit enemies patrol near the entrance, so dispose of them, enter the ruin, and fight another bandit inside. Near the first intersection, the inhabitants have been creative with one of the ancient fire traps and a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") will slowly cook when it activates. The path straight ahead is hindered by said fire trap and a leveled lock. For a better chance of a surprise attack, take the eastern tunnel and kill a few bandits along the way. Down the last set of stairs is where [Alain Dufont](/wiki/Skyrim:Alain_Dufont "Skyrim:Alain Dufont") resides, so consider entering [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") mode as you descend. There's a group of three bandits in the chamber and a fourth bandit hidden behind the southern gate. There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Oil_Slicks.2FOil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Traps") on the ground that you may take advantage of by using a fire spell to roast the opposition, the unarmored Alain included. Fighting them normally is also an option, but beware of Alain's weapon of choice, the unique and enchanted warhammer [Aegisbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Aegisbane "Skyrim:Aegisbane"). When Alain is dead, the quest will update. Return to Muiri or, if you have yet to optionally kill Nilsine and still wish to do so, head to Windhelm.

### Reward

When you return to Muiri in Markarth, she will show no remorse whatsoever and will hand you gold for taking care of her ex-lover. If you chose to kill Nilsine Shatter-Shield, you will receive a leveled amount of gold and the unique [Muiri's Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Muiri's Ring") which boosts the strength of potions by 15%. Otherwise, you will only receive 100 gold. Completing the optional objective will also allow you to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") Muiri. Back in the Sanctuary, Astrid will thank you for a job well done and proceed to show greater paranoia concerning [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") and his insanity. She will finish the quest by asking you to do her a favor, starting the next quest [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark").

## Notes

- This quest was originally meant to play out quite differently. Instead of being found in Raldbthar, Alain Dufont was meant to be present in a jail cell inside of the Windhelm Barracks. Early dialogue for Muiri shows that the original objective for the quest was just to kill Alain, while the optional objective was to kill him during a Pit match in the unused Windhelm arena, in which he would've been an opponent. The role Nilsine would've played, if any, is unknown.
- If you haven't already received the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") and [Blank Lexicon](/wiki/Skyrim:Blank_Lexicon "Skyrim:Blank Lexicon") from [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus"), it is convenient to do so before killing Dufont. By doing so you can complete your quest objective, obtain entry to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), and also obtain one of the [Aetherium Shards](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard") without having to make multiple trips through [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar").
- In the room with Alain Dufont and the two bandits, two [Dwemer ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista") aim down from the ledge above. The one on the right is aimed at Alain, while the one on the left is aimed at the bandits.
- If you have already killed Alain before first meeting Muiri, then you cannot get the optional quest to kill Nilsine.
  -  After receiving the initial quest from Astrid, use the console command `setstage DB03 30` to add the objective to kill Nilsine and `setstage DB03 40` to add the objective to return to Muiri with news of Alain's death. Return to Muiri and she should give you the optional reward as well.

## Bugs

- As soon as the quest is initiated, you can talk to Nilsine and tell her you have been sent by Muiri, even though that is not yet the case.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Alain Dufont's initial dialogue cuts off before you are allowed to give a response and he enters combat before he's supposed to.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, addresses this issue. It was incorrectly set as a goodbye response, and the script never should have been added to it.
- It is possible that, after the first set of contracts, Cicero never shows up at the Falkreath Sanctuary, so no further quests will be available.
  -  This can be fixed by using the console command `Setstage` to complete all the stages of Mourning Never Comes and to start Whispers in the Dark until asked to eavesdrop on Cicero.
  -  It can also be fixed by using the console command `Setstage` to set the stage of *this* quest to 5 while outside the sanctuary. After doing that, entering the sanctuary will trigger the scene with Cicero having arrived. After the discussion with Astrid and the others, Astrid will speak to the player and hand over the contract for Muiri.
  -  If you killed Alain Dufont before starting this quest, he can be resurrected by the console commands `prid 000d2aff` and `resurrect`. Entering the Falkreath Sanctuary afterward should trigger Cicero's arrival.
- If Nilsine dies before the quest is started, no matter the cause, Muiri will reward you her ring as if you killed Nilsine. After the quest, Tova will commit suicide and Torbjorn will mention their deaths as usual.

## Quest Stages

| Mourning Never Comes (DB03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | *Objective 5:* Speak with Astrid |
| 10 |  | Astrid has given me my first major contract. I am to contact Muiri, the apothecary's assistant in The Hag's Cure, in Markarth. Muiri has apparently performed the Black Sacrament, and is trying to contact the Dark Brotherhood. *Objective 10:* Talk to Muiri |
| 20 |  | Muiri wants me to kill the bandit leader Alain Dufont, who is holed up with his gang of cutthroats in the dwarven ruin of Raldbthar. If Dufont dies, the contract will be completed, but Muiri will pay me some kind of bonus if I also eliminate Nilsine Shatter-Shield, in Windhelm. *Objective 20:* Kill Alain Dufont |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* (Optional) Kill Nilsine Shatter-Shield |
| 40 |  | Alain Dufont is dead. I must now return to Markarth, and tell Muiri the deed is complete. *Objective 40:* Talk to Muiri |
| 50 |  | I have spoken to Muiri, and been paid for the assassination of Alain Dufont. I must now report back to Astrid at the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary. *Objective 50:* Report back to Astrid |
| 200 | ☑ | After contacting Muiri, the apothecary's assistant at the Hag's Cure in Markarth, I learned that she wished to hire the Dark Brotherhood to kill a slanderous ex-lover. I killed the man, the bandit leader Alain Dufont, and was rewarded for the contract. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 25, 31, 35, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB03`.

Movarth's Lair

**Movarth's Lair** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") led by [Movarth Piquine](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth_Piquine "Skyrim:Movarth Piquine"). It contains only one zone, *[Movarth's Lair](#Movarth.27s_Lair)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

A twisting path runs all the way from the north side of Morthal to the cave. There are two patches of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") near the entrance, one of which can only be picked by carefully approaching the lit brazier to the right, as moving too close to the entrance will trigger entry. There is a skull on the stones to the left.

### Movarth's Lair

The entry tunnel leads to a wooden platform over a room with two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). There is a ramp to the left that descends into the chamber. There is nothing else of interest in this first room, except the dark tunnel to the south which leads to another room, where a [vampire's thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall") is sitting at a table with a lantern. Beyond the thrall, along a short twisting path, is a small room with three carts filled with the remains of a few people, and an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") growing in the middle of the room. There is a hole in the rock wall to the left, but it is too high to reach.

The path deeper into the network of caverns is to the north of where the vampire's thrall sat. Another vampire's thrall is working in this room, burying corpses in a hole in the northwest portion of the room. There are three piles of rocks around the room littered with remains. There is a table to the left of the entrance with some generic clothes, another to the right with more generic clothes, and a bleeding crown growing at the base of the second table. By the western wall is a cart and a table with more clothes. By this table is a pickaxe, a barrel with a potion of minor magicka, and beyond that a bleeding crown. The corpses of three [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") and a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redguard (dead)") lie in the hole, and the only thing of note is that the Redguard carries a lockpick. Lastly, on the other side of the room, there is a bedroll and another bleeding crown.

The next tunnel is to the north, and splits into a higher and lower pathway. The higher path is bridged with wooden planks, and there is an iron ore vein in the wall. This path leads around the wall to a bedroom of sorts. The lower path leads to the main chamber, where the master vampire and one of his followers are feasting. If stage 100 of the quest [Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest") has been reached, the former will be Movarth Piquine; otherwise, it will be a generic vampire boss. There are three other branches from the main chamber: one to the northeast (where you can find the second iron ore vein), one to the east, and one to the south. There is a vampire in the tunnel to the south, and another in the tunnel to the northeast, who will detect any hostilities in the main room and rush to their master's aid.

There isn't much in the main room. The table is covered with food and drink, with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two small coin purses, and a fair bit of loose gold. The table also holds an enchanter's potion, as well as remains of the vampires' victims, clothes, armor, bones, etc. Lastly, there are two [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") growing between the table and the southern tunnel.

The tunnel to the northeast leads to the other side of the bedroom area that the higher wooden path lead to. There are two imp stools growing in the northeast tunnel. The room is split in two: one part with a single bed, and another section with three bedrolls. By the single bed is a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")*, [Movarth's boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Movarth's Boots") (which provide a 15% sneaking bonus), and a shelf with a large assortment of boots (which includes a pair of [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots") and a pair of [Stormcloak officer boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Boots "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Boots")). The only item of note by the bedrolls is a potion of minor healing on a dresser.

Behind Movarth's throne to the east in the main chamber is a wooden ramp to a small room with another vampire. There is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") here, along with a set of shelves holding a potion of healing and a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, a book about Movarth.

The tunnel to the south leads to one final room. There is a vampire's thrall on the platform to the left. To the right is a wooden platform with a bedroll, a chest, and a leveled poison on a dresser. At the top of the stone ramp is another imp stool, with a large coin purse, a bow, and a few leveled arrows on the cobweb-covered table to the left. A tunnel to the right leads to the opening above the small room with the three carts filled with remains, providing a convenient return to the entrance.

## Notes

- [Alva](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva "Skyrim:Alva") will appear in the bedroom area of the cave if you did not kill her during the quest Laid to Rest. She will engage the other vampires in combat.
  - Don't kill Alva in the cave, or that will count as a crime, and [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar")'s disposition towards you will drop to -2.
- By default, Movarth's appearance is randomly-generated. With the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on, he will always appear as a Nord.
- According to a [Development Map](/wiki/File:SR-map-Development_Map_02.png "File:SR-map-Development Map 02.png"), this location was originally called **Ghoruun Hall**. References to "Ghoruun" still appear multiple times in the final game data, most often in scripts tied to the quest. Moreover, the original vampire master inhabiting the hall was apparently intended to be a different NPC named **Morgus Ghoruun**, who was either changed into or replaced by Movarth in the final game.

## Bugs

- Movarth's Lair cannot be marked as cleared, as none of its inhabitants are tagged as a boss.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  If you want to update the "cleared" status, enter the following command in the console: `SetLocationCleared 0001BDFC 1`
- The fix from Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.3.2 created a new bug, as the "boss" vampires it introduced did not respawn and may therefore break radiant quests.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- During the quest, once you kill Movarth and make your way out of the cave, [Helgi's Ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgi%27s_Ghost "Skyrim:Helgi's Ghost") begins speaking her dialogue line immediately, and attempting to speak with her and initiate the only available dialogue line about avenging her and her mother causes her to stop speaking and disappear. It can be assumed that she was supposed to have a forcegreet, and the available dialogue option was supposed to trigger her dialogue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. The line of dialogue they had her able to use should not have been enabled since you can't use it until she's begun her hello line anyway, and that hello line is what disables her.
- Using the ramp in the corridor leading to the main boss chamber can cause your follower to briefly be stuck, then disappear and return to the previous room due to a broken navmesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- If Alva is killed here during the quest, [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar")'s and [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami")'s dispositions towards you will take a big hit, and fall to -2.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- If you shoot Movarth undetected, he may run and eventually get stuck in a wall where you cannot hit him. Leaving and reentering the dungeon will reset him to his initial position in his chair. **?**
- A crash may occur when approaching the lair for the quest [Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Totems of Hircine"). **?**

## Maps

- 

  Movarth's Lair

# Skyrim:My Pet Elytra (Dementia)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

| **Save a young Elytra from the Seducer bandits.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Seducers Bandit's Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Seducers_Bandit%27s_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Seducers Bandit's Cage Key") |

.jpg)

A smuggled Demented Elytra Nymph

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Locate the Seducer's Bandit Camp.
2. Free the Elytra Nymph from its cage.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest is part of the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") quest bundle, and can be completed during the [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power") quest.

In the Seducers Bandit Camp northwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), there is a large cage with a [Demented Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph") pet. Nearby is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_Demented_Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Note on Demented Elytra Nymph"), as well as a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Seducers_Bandit%27s_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Seducers Bandit's Cage Key") inside of a chest.

The Elytra Nymph's cage will open when either the lock to its cage is picked or the key is used.

Once the Elytra Nymph is free, speak to it and invite it to come with you. The Elytra Nymph will agree to follow you, and the quest will end.

## Bugs

- At the end of the quest to get the Elytra pet for the Mania version, the dialogue to accept it as a follower is incorrectly checking for Stage 50 in the quest for the Dementia version - this stage doesn't exist, and isn't the right quest to check either. It should be checking for Stage 25 on the Mania quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_ElytraPetAcquisition_Dementia stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_ElytraPetAcquisition_Dementia`.

# Skyrim:My Pet Elytra (Mania)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Save a young Elytra from the Saints bandits.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Saints Bandit's Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit%27s_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Saints Bandit's Cage Key") |
| Location(s): | Saints Bandit's camp (unmarked) |
| Reward: | [Manic Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph") pet |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_ElytraPetAcquisition\_Mania |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |
| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Concurrent | [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power") | | |

.jpg)

A smuggled Manic Elytra Nymph

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Free the Elytra Nymph.

## Detailed Walkthrough

To begin the quest you must find the [Saints Bandit's Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit%27s_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Saints Bandit's Cage Key"). It is located in a chest found in the Saints Bandit camp just to the west of [North Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:North Brittleshin Pass"). This is the first Saints bandit camp you encounter during the quest [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power").

Once you have the key, you can open the cage and talk to the [Manic Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph") inside. Accept it as your pet and the quest will end, granting you the spell [Teleport Pet: Manic Elytra Nymph](/wiki/Skyrim:Teleport_Pet:_Manic_Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Teleport Pet: Manic Elytra Nymph").

## Bugs

- At the end of the quest to get the Elytra pet for Mania, the dialogue to accept it as a follower is incorrectly checking for Stage 50 in the quest for the Dementia version - this stage doesn't exist, and isn't the right quest to check either. It should be checking for Stage 25 on the Mania quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 0:* Free the Elytra Nymph |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 17, 19, 20, 25, 30, 40, 50, 60, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_ElytraPetAcquisition_Mania stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_ElytraPetAcquisition_Mania`.

# Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") |
| Location(s): | [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") |
| Reward: | [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE010\_PetPurchaseQuest |
| Added by: | [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab") |

Spot the Mudcrab hiding in the floor

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest no longer appears in your journal following the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update.

1. Read a [notice of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Dwarven_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Dwarven Mudcrab").
2. Buy a mudcrab from [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").

**Note**: You can also steal [notice of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Dwarven_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Dwarven Mudcrab") from Calcemo to acquire ownership and the associated spell. This works on unpatched versions, such as the Nintendo Switch.

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. The mudcrab can still be purchased from [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").**

Once you've installed the Dwarven Armored Mudcrab Creation, you will receive this quest and a [notice of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Dwarven_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Dwarven Mudcrab"), which directs you to talk to Calcelmo in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep").

Travel to Understone Keep in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and meet Calcelmo in the ruins section of the keep. From him, you'll be able to purchase the [ownership deed](/wiki/Skyrim:Ownership_Deed_-_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Ownership Deed - Mudcrab"). Once you've done so, you'll find the [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)") beside the arcane enchanter. You'll also receive a [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Teleport_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Teleport Pet Mudcrab") that teaches you a spell to [teleport the mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Teleport_Pet:_Dwarven_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Teleport Pet: Dwarven Mudcrab") to you.

The mudcrab serves as an animal follower, with the added ability to carry items and allow you to send it to specific locations.

## Quest Stages

| My Pet Mudcrab () | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | I've received a Notice of Sale from Calcelmo. I should read it and see what it's about. *Objective 0:* Read Notice of Sale |
| 10 |  | Calcelmo has found a Dwarven Armored Mudcrab during his excavations, and has offered to sell him to me. I should head to Understone Keep to speak with him, and purchase the Mudcrab. *Objective 10:* Purchase the Mudcrab |
| 20 |  | I've purchased a Pet Dwarven Mudcrab from Calcelmo. I should talk to him, and either send him to his new home, or bring him with me. *Objective 20:* Meet your new pet |
| 30 | ☑ | Calcelmo found a Dwarven Armored Mudcrab during his excavations, and offered to sell him to me. I obliged, and now keep him as a pet, who I can bring with me, or send to any of my homes, or main cities. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage quest stage`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest, and `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest quest`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest.

# Skyrim:My Pet Nix-Hound

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Buy a tame [nix-hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Revus Sarvani](/wiki/Skyrim:Revus_Sarvani "Skyrim:Revus Sarvani") or [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") |
| Location(s): | [Revus Sarvani](/wiki/Skyrim:Revus_Sarvani "Skyrim:Revus Sarvani")'s camp or [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") |
| Reward: | Pet [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE035\_PetAcquireQuest |
| Required Items: | 400 [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") |
| Added by: | [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound") |

The tame nix-hound at Revus Sarvani's camp

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [notice of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Nix-Hound").
2. Buy a nix-hound from [Revus Sarvani](/wiki/Skyrim:Revus_Sarvani "Skyrim:Revus Sarvani") or [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri").

## Detailed Walkthrough

**Note: This quest was originally added to your journal upon installing the [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). With the release of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition"), this quest no longer appears in your journal. The Nix-Hound can still be acquired from Revus.**

Once you've installed the [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Nix-Hound") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you will receive this quest and a [notice of sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Nix-Hound_(Revus) "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Nix-Hound (Revus)"), which directs you to talk to [Revus Sarvani](/wiki/Skyrim:Revus_Sarvani "Skyrim:Revus Sarvani") at his camp west of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). Revus is not an essential NPC, so it is possible to kill him prior to installing this Creation. If this occurs, you will instead receive a [different notice](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice_of_Sale_-_Nix-Hound_(Geldis) "Skyrim:Notice of Sale - Nix-Hound (Geldis)") directing you to [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") at [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

Travel to Solstheim and locate the specified NPC. Offer to purchase the nix-hound for 400 gold and you will be given a [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Teleport_Pet_Nix-Hound "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Teleport Pet Nix-Hound") that teaches you a spell to teleport the nix-hound to you. You will be directed to introduce yourself to the nearby nix-hound to complete the quest. It will now serve as an animal follower, with the added ability to carry items, provide you with random [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), or be sent to wait at a specific city or player house.

## Notes

- The Nix-Hound Creation also adds enemy nix-hounds to the wilds of Solstheim.
- The pet Nix-Hound behaves identically to other [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") pets, such as the [mudcrab pet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)") added by the [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab") Creation.
- The Nix-Hound can be purchased by speaking directly to the Nix-Hound instead of Revus.

## Bugs

- It may be impossible to purchase the pet Nix-Hound in some non-English languages.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.640, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| My Pet Nix-Hound () | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've received a Notice of Sale from Solstheim. I should read it and see what it's about. *Objective 0 or 1:* Read the Notice of Sale *or* Read the Notice of Sale |
| 20 |  | A tamed Nix-Hound is for sale on Solstheim, which could be useful to me. I should consider purchasing it. *Objective 5:* Travel to Solstheim |
| 25 |  | A tamed Nix-Hound is for sale on Solstheim, which could be useful to me. I should consider purchasing it. *Objective 10 or 15:* Purchase the Nix-Hound *or* Purchase the Nix-Hound |
| 30 |  | I've purchased a tamed Nix-Hound. I should meet it and bring it with me. *Objective 20:* Meet the Nix-Hound |
| 40 | ☑ | I've purchased a tamed Nix-Hound on Solstheim. I can bring it with me, ask it to carry items, or send it to any of my homes. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage quest stage`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest, and `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest quest`, where `quest` is the internal name of the quest.

# Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Myrwatch

**Myrwatch** is a mage tower player home east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). It contains two zones connected by portal, *[Myrwatch](#Myrwatch)* and *[Myrwatch Gallery](#Myrwatch_Gallery)*.

The tower was built in the [Third Era](/wiki/Lore:Third_Era "Lore:Third Era") by rogue mages from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), and closely resembles College architecture. The bottom level has beds for your [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") and [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption").

## Related Quests

- **[Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch"): Locate and enter a mysterious tower.

### Exterior

The tower is built partially in the water, with a small bridge crossing over to a narrow stretch of swampy land. The body of [Hans](/wiki/Skyrim:Hans "Skyrim:Hans") lies against a tree stump to the north, next to an [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), and *[Sindnar's Tower Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sindnar%27s_Tower_Notes "Skyrim:Sindnar's Tower Notes")*. A leveled [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") guards this area and presumably killed Hans.

The bridge has a seal depicting the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus"). When you light it with a fire spell, the door to the tower unlocks and the magic beacon nearby is lit.

The main chamber

### Myrwatch

The main chamber is divided into a central area and two side areas. The central area is dominated by an open fireplace. A piece of [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") can be found on a table against the left wall; maps of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") are posted above, to the left is a [Shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrines"). The right wall includes a table holding the ordinary book *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")* and a display case in the bookshelf containing a [glass dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), [flawless emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Emerald "Skyrim:Flawless Emerald"), [flawless sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire"), and Ring of Illusion. [*Anora's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Anora%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Anora's Journal") lies on a table here.

The side area right of the door has two bookshelves you can fill, two beds, and a chest above the bookshelf farther from the door. In the back of the chamber, there is a long dining table flanked by a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on the right and an [oven](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking") on the left. The side area left of the door is more interesting. Just left of the oven is a small display area, with a mannequin, weapon plaque, safe, and chest. A double bed splits the side area in two, above the bed is a [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrines"). Left of this is a portal to the gallery above and farther left is another empty bookshelf. On the inner wall across from the bookshelf is a [Cure Disease Potion Recipe](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease_Potion_Recipe "Skyrim:Cure Disease Potion Recipe").

Myrwatch Gallery

### Myrwatch Gallery

Activate the portal and you'll be transported to another circular chamber. A large glowing blue orb hangs from the ceiling. The gallery is a crafting and display room. Immediately in front of you is a green [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). Just above it is a [grand soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem") and a holder for [Saerek's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerek%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Saerek's Skull Key") and [Torsten's Skull Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten%27s_Skull_Key "Skyrim:Torsten's Skull Key"). A number of smaller soul gems, the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*, and a [Spell Tome: Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Sparks "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Sparks") sit on the enchanter table.

The center of the gallery has an alchemy garden on the near side and an equipment crafting area opposite it. The garden has eleven empty plots of [Fertile Soil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil") for gardening, and many more plants in between these. The crafting area consists of a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), smelting pot (same as a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter")), and the "[All Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:All_Forge "Skyrim:All Forge")". The All Forge functions identically to a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), but allows for crafting of items usually restricted to the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") and [Gunmar's forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge#Smithing_Forges "Skyrim:Forge"). A variety of relevant materials sit on the shelves above.

A multitude of displays can be found as you move counterclockwise from the portal. The first wall has three weapon plaques and a display case. Two mannequins flank the second wall; in the middle are weapon plaques and racks designed to hold [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") items: [Champion's Cudgel](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Cudgel "Skyrim:Champion's Cudgel") and [Bloodskal Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Blade "Skyrim:Bloodskal Blade") above and [Glass Bow of the Stag Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow_of_the_Stag_Prince "Skyrim:Glass Bow of the Stag Prince"), [Soulrender](/wiki/Skyrim:Soulrender "Skyrim:Soulrender"), [Bloodscythe](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodscythe "Skyrim:Bloodscythe"), and [Dwarven Black Bow of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate") below. The inner side of the next section has an extremely rare [staff enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_Enchanter "Skyrim:Staff Enchanter"), with six [heart stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") on the shelves behind it and unenchanted illusion and destruction staves in a basket on the ground. The outer wall opposite the enchanter has two more mannequins and two weapon plaques between them.

Continuing counterclockwise, the next section has two display cases on the inner wall as well as two mannequins and five weapon plaques on the outer wall. The fifth wall right of the portal has a row of holders for each [bug in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"); a weapon plaque is posted on the inner and outer walls and the inner wall has a grand total of six weapon racks lining it. The next wall, directly across from the portal, features the same setup as [Tundra Homestead](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead_(place) "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead (place)") for the [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Masks "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Masks") (i.e. a bust for each mask aside from [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(item) "Skyrim:Miraak (item)")).

Six more weapon racks and a single weapon plaque line the next inner wall, across from which are racks for staves: the [Skull of Corruption](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_of_Corruption "Skyrim:Skull of Corruption"), [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack"), [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod"), [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus"), and [Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Jyrik_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Staff of Jyrik Gauldurson"). A wooden panel above these holds daggers: the [Blade of Woe](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Woe "Skyrim:Blade of Woe"), [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang"), [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane"), [Blade of Sacrifice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade_of_Sacrifice "Skyrim:Blade of Sacrifice"), [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor"), and [Keening](/wiki/Skyrim:Keening "Skyrim:Keening"). The next section, now the fourth left of the portal, has two more display cases on the inner wall, two mannequins on the outer wall, and between the mannequins four plaques meant to hold the [Shield of Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Ysgramor "Skyrim:Shield of Ysgramor"), [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"), [Spellbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellbreaker "Skyrim:Spellbreaker"), [Targe of the Blooded](/wiki/Skyrim:Targe_of_the_Blooded "Skyrim:Targe of the Blooded"), and [Aetherial Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Shield "Skyrim:Aetherial Shield").

An alchemy lab sits at the end of the inner wall. Dozens of ingredients and potions are scattered on the table and shelves, most notably two samples of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") and one of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"). An expensive [deadly recovery poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadly_Recovery_Poison "Skyrim:Deadly Recovery Poison") sits atop the shelf. Across from the lab are two additional mannequins guarding plaques for [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") items: [Dawnguard Rune Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Shield"), [Harkon's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Harkon%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Harkon's Sword"), [Dawnguard Rune Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Axe"), and [Dawnguard Rune Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Hammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Hammer"). The penultimate wall holds a plaque for [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"); holders for the five [paragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Unique_Items "Skyrim:Other Unique Items") sit below, beside static cupboards on which you can place the [Initiate's Ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") and [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield"). The final wall has three generic weapon plaques and a display case.

## Bugs

- Both the leveled chaurus enemy and *[Sindnar's Tower Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sindnar%27s_Tower_Notes "Skyrim:Sindnar's Tower Notes")* respawn.
- Many of the items in Myrwatch Gallery have a tendency to fall over or fly off their shelves upon entering the area.
- The staff enchanter in Myrwatch is bugged and grants 20 times the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") experience it is supposed to. This is due to the staff enchanter in Tel Mithryn having a hidden perk (`DLC2StaffEnchantingMult`) that reduces the experience gained by 95%; the staff enchanter in Myrwatch has a different Editor ID and thus is unaffected by the perk.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.318, fixes this bug.
- A section of the water surrounding the path outside clips through the ground.
- The strongbox on the arcane enchanter table is not safe for storage. **?**
- Placing some dragon priest masks on its respective pedestal may cause it to disappear.
- The weapon plaques are heavily bugged, removing weapons may result in the plaque activators deactivating. This can be fixed by using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `resetinterior ccEEJSSE002MageTowerSecond`, make sure to remove all weapons in advance, or they'll be lost after the reset.
- Weapons loaded into plaques may appear floating in mid-air in random angles rather than appear in their proper place.
- Your child or a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") may sometimes end up underground when spawning outside the house. Leaving the cell will resolve this.
- When saving the game, picking up an item in Myrwatch and reloading the save, the item has disappeared from Myrwatch and is not in the inventory.
- On the Bugs in a Jar displays it incorrectly say "Firefly" instead of "Torchbug"
- Keening may fall off its holder each time you enter the gallery. **?**
- The urn on the enchanting table is not safe to store items in for longer than 3-4 game days. **?**
- When selecting this location for home after adopting a child, the child may remain where they are originally found and will only repeat the dialogue of gathering their things, rendering interacting with the adopted child impossible. Rarely, their dialogue will act as if they've arrived at the home (while still in the cell in which they're originally found), but the child cannot be spoken to beyond this point. Attempting to adopt a second child will cause dialogue to exit out by itself before fully adopting the second child.
- If you kill Astrid during the quest [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") and loot her body for the Blade of Woe, it cannot be placed in the holder.
- Adopting more than one child for a family at Myrwatch will cause one of the children to sometimes fail to go to sleep. Since children at Myrwatch will try to sleep on the closest child bed, if both children are closer to one of the beds, only one can sleep, the other will stand all night.
- One of the large bookcase shelves only holds 6 books instead of 12.
- The Spider Control Rod is unable to go on its respective plaque. **?**

## Overview

A chaurus guards Myrwatch

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)") and take [*Hans's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Hans%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hans's Journal") from [Hans](/wiki/Skyrim:Hans "Skyrim:Hans").
2. Read the journal and cast a [fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") spell at the seal.
3. Enter the tower to complete the quest.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest automatically begins upon approaching [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)"), an undiscovered tower marked on your map. The tower is just east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and is guarded by a lone leveled [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). You will need to attempt to open the locked front entrance in order to update the quest.

The body of [Hans](/wiki/Skyrim:Hans "Skyrim:Hans") can be found nearby. Loot his body and read [*Hans's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Hans%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hans's Journal") to learn how to gain entrance to the tower. The journal provides a hint in this regard:

:   *"When the eye is doused in flames, the hair*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *will light the way."*

You will need to cast a [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") spell at the eye-shaped seal on the ground in front of the entrance. Helpfully, Hans can also be looted for a copy of [Spell Tome: Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Flames "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Flames") in case you have no fire damage spells. Once you cast the spell, the [ghostly apparition](/wiki/Skyrim:Elianora "Skyrim:Elianora") of a rabbit will appear (or more than likely a hare, per the hint in the journal). The apparition will proceed to hop over to the nearby magical brazier and will cause it to alight with a tower of blue energy. You will then receive a message stating that *"The tower door was unlocked by mysterious forces."*

Head inside the tower to complete the quest and investigate your new [player home](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses").

## Notes

- This quest would originally be added to your journal upon installing the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This was changed with the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update, allowing you to discover the location through natural gameplay.
  - Myrwatch will still be marked on your map as an undiscovered location from the start of the game, a legacy of the original quest design.

## Quest Stages

| Myrwatch (ccEEJSSE002\_MageTowerQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | I've heard rumors of a mysterious tower somewhere east of Morthal. If it's abandoned, I may be able to make of use of it. When I reached the tower, I found a journal that may provide clues on how to enter it. *Objective 5:* Read Hans's journal |
| 10 |  | I've heard rumors of a mysterious tower somewhere east of Morthal. If it's abandoned, I may be able to make of use of it. *Objective 10:* Investigate Myrwatch |
| 20 |  | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. However, the door to tower is locked. I should investigate the area to see if there's a way in. *Objective 20:* Find a way inside the tower |
| 30 |  | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. However, the door to tower is locked. A journal on a nearby body indicates I need to activate a stone seal to light the way. *Objective 30:* Activate the seal |
| 40 |  | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. However, the door to tower is locked. A journal on a nearby body indicates I need to activate a stone seal. Activating it summoned a ghostly apparition. I should follow it and see where it leads. *Objective 40:* Follow the hare |
| 50 |  | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. However, the door to tower is locked. A journal on a nearby body indicates I need to activate a stone seal. Activating it summoned a ghostly apparition which unlocked the tower. |
| 60 |  | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. Activating a seal by the front door summoned a ghostly apparition which unlocked the tower. *Objective 60:* Enter Myrwatch |
| 100 | ☑ | I've found a mysterious tower in the swamps of Hjaalmarch. After finding my way inside, it appears to be an elaborate home built for a powerful mage. I may be able to make use of the lodgings in my travels through Skyrim. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEEJSSE002_MageTowerQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEEJSSE002_MageTowerQuest`.

# Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Camp: Mythic Dawn Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mythic+Dawn+Camp)) | | |
| Added by | [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Unknown [(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data") | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |

Mythic Dawn Camp

**Mythic Dawn Camp** is an expedition camp for the Mythic Dawn to reopen the ruins of [Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle"), added by [The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") creation. The camp is located on the southern slopes of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), west of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and north of the [Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack").

It can be reached by traveling from the Alchemist's Shack or [Honeystrand Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Cave "Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave"), by taking a mountain path that connects the two. The path leads uphill to a large flat snow-covered area. Before the camp appears, the path and plateau are nothing more than an alternate route past the bear at Honeystrand Cave, and when traveling from the southwestern end you will encounter a leveled [Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"), which you must kill or calm to proceed.

Several Mythic Dawn cultists and their tents appear here once stage 60 of the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)") is reached, and they must be defeated in order to reach the tent and find the *[Excavation Leader's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Excavation_Leader%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Excavation Leader's Journal")*; the journal explains that an excavation mission is being carried out in the mountains to the south, and updates your map with the marker for [Varlais Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Varlais_Cavern "Skyrim:Varlais Cavern") if you have not already discovered it. The quest will then direct the Dragonborn to the entrance of the Ayleid Ruin of [Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle") that the excavation team has been digging to from the Skyrim side.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Investigate the activities of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") cult.

## Notes

- There is no map marker for this place, even after it appears during the related quest. This can make it more difficult to find.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Camp&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Mzinchaleft

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png) | Dwarven Ruin: Mzinchaleft ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzinchaleft)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Mzinchaleft "Lore:Mzinchaleft")) | | |
| # of Zones | 3 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 16 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Dwarven Automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MzinchaleftExterior, Mzinchaleft01, Mzinchaleft02, Mzinchaleft03 | |
