### Wolfskull Cave Necromancers

These four necromancers are found accompanying the [Ritual Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Ritual_Master "Skyrim:Ritual Master") at [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") during [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf"). The group includes a Breton woman (0009655b), a Dunmer woman (000e1036), a Nord woman (000e1037), and a Nord man (000e1049). They will have the same leveled stats as a generic necromancer of the appropriate level, but are all named "Necromancer".

## Named Necromancers

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Arondil](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil") | [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild") | An Altmer man exiled from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") for experimenting on the dead |
| [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") | [Ansilvund Burial Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Burial_Chambers "Skyrim:Ansilvund Burial Chambers") | A Redguard woman who commands an army of [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") after failing to resurrect her husband |
| [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran") | [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") | The mage responsible for the corruption of [Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia "Skyrim:Meridia")'s temple |
| [Nimphaneth](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimphaneth "Skyrim:Nimphaneth") | [Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave") | A Bosmer cannibal encountered during [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") |
| [Sanyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanyon "Skyrim:Sanyon") | Reachcliff Cave | An Altmer cannibal encountered during The Taste of Death |
| [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") | [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") | A Dunmer woman trapped in Southfringe Sanctum seeking to escape and find her daughter |
| [Vals Veran](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") | [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb") | A Dunmer attempting to raise [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir")'s ancestors |

## Related Quests

- **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").
- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").
- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Let Sleeping Wolves Lie](/wiki/Skyrim:Let_Sleeping_Wolves_Lie "Skyrim:Let Sleeping Wolves Lie")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf"): Stop a necromancer from raising undead wolf minions.
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").
- **[The Savior of Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri")**: Help a necromancer escape from [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").
- **[The Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:The Staff of Hasedoki")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki"): Locate a legendary staff that's been smuggled into Skyrim.
- **[Toying With The Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead")**: Retrieve a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil")'s journals for an interested buyer.

### World Interactions

- **[Necromancers Attack Player](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Necromancers_Attack_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- Most necromancers have a [morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") of "Any Crime", which means they're willing to commit any crime. The necromancers found at Wolfskull Cave, however, have a morality of "No Crime," which means they are unwilling to commit crimes of any sort. Their aggression is still very high, though, so they will attack you on sight regardless.
- All the generic necromancers that are Bretons are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means necromancers are slightly more likely to be Breton than one of the other races.
- With the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, necromancers can often be found in the company of hostile [Bonewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonewolf "Skyrim:Bonewolf").
- If you have the [Necromantic Grimoire](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromantic_Grimoire "Skyrim:Necromantic Grimoire") Creation installed, Arch Necromancers will be wearing a [Elite Necromancer Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Necromancer_Hood "Skyrim:Elite Necromancer Hood") and [Elite Necromancer Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Necromancer_Robes "Skyrim:Elite Necromancer Robes"), which can be looted from them. [*verification needed — unsure about other leveled necromancers and if pickpocketing is an option*]

### Books

- ***[Ivara's Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivara%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Ivara's Notes")*** by [Ivara of Olenveld](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivara_of_Olenveld "Skyrim:Ivara of Olenveld") — Journal of a necromancer hoping to gain power from the Ideal Masters [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki")
- ***[Necromancer's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Journal_(Bone_Wolf) "Skyrim:Necromancer's Journal (Bone Wolf)")*** — A necromancer binds an undead wolf to his service [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf")

- ***[Necromancer's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Necromancer's Letter")*** — A letter about Necromancers taking over Fort Snowhawk

# Skyrim:Nepos's House

## Overview

Nepos's House

**Nepos's House** is a luxurious private residence owned by [Nepos the Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos_the_Nose "Skyrim:Nepos the Nose"), who is a wealthy resident of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). It is located on the third terrace on the northern side of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), next door to [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"), above [Endon's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Endon's House") and two terraces above [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company").

His three [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") servants appear to be very protective of him, especially [Uaile](/wiki/Skyrim:Uaile "Skyrim:Uaile"), who questions visitors at the door and claims to be Nepos's maid.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Nepos the Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos_the_Nose "Skyrim:Nepos the Nose") (Owner)  [Morven](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven "Skyrim:Morven") (Servant)  [Tynan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tynan "Skyrim:Tynan") (Servant)  [Uaile](/wiki/Skyrim:Uaile "Skyrim:Uaile") (Servant) |

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Nepos's House

It is a large single-story property that is lavishly furnished. There are numerous [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and sacks throughout the property, along with plenty of fancy cookware. The main room has two stone tables with wooden chairs down the middle of the room, laden with four portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), plenty of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), five [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), many pieces of cheese, two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

There is a dresser with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") on top against the south wall. To the right, in the southwestern corner, is a round wooden table and two chairs with a large coin purse, a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), and a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on top. Against the west wall is a cupboard holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a couple of loaves of bread, a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). To the right of this is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a set of shelves to its right of that. These shelves hold a bottle of wine, a couple of pieces of cheese, and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). Beside the shelves is a small square table with clutter on top. In the northwestern corner is a door into a bedroom. Along the north wall is a stone bench, a couple of wooden chairs, and a stone shelf holding a loaf of bread. In the northeastern corner is door to another room. Against the east wall is a stone table with a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a thistle branch, a basket containing a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and another basket containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"). To the right of the table is a piece of loose [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top of a food barrel. In the southeast corner is a large fireplace with a pile of firewood to the left. To the right is a goat cheese wheel in a cast iron pot and in front is a wooden chair. Above the wood is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Against the south wall is a kettle holding a cabbage, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a potato, with another rack above it holding two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a garlic braid, and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

The bedroom to the northwest contains two single owned beds both coming out from the north wall, separated by an end table with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. To the left of the beds is a chair and against the west wall is a tall wardrobe and a dresser, both containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). On the dresser is a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and a green apple. There is also a small square wooden table against a wall to the southwest with another green apple and mead barrel on top. Finally against the east wall is a set of shelves holding a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum").

Through the other door is a kitchen area in front of you and, on a raised section, another sleeping area. In the middle of the room is another stone table with a wooden chair at either end. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a portion of grilled leeks, a raw rabbit leg, a seared slaughterfish, a carrot, two loaves of bread, a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), and several pieces of cheese. Behind the table, on the rear wall is a large fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front. On your right as you enter, on a stone shelf is an apprentice-locked display cabinet with an [enchanted steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"). The display cabinet can be unlocked with the [key to Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Nepos's House") which is carried by all the residents. Against the east wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [draught of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Draught of Extra Magicka"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a couple of pieces of cheese, and a potato in a cast iron pot. To the right of the shelves is a wash basin and beside this on the floor is a basket containing two cabbages and several potatoes. In the northeast corner is a small square stone table with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and an unlocked chest, with a basket under the table containing two gourds and a potato.

At the western end of the room are stairs up between two shoulder-high walls, to the raised section. On the partition walls is a bowl containing an empty [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem"), a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), and a wooden bowl containing five [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins. On the raised section are two owned beds; the first coming out from the south wall is a single and the other coming out from the west wall is a large double. To the right of the single is a tall wardrobe with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") to the left of it and in an open crate, on top of another crate are four [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"). There are end tables on either side of the double bed. On the left-hand one is a copy of *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")* with a stone shelf to the left holding three more common books and a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, Part 4")*. On the right-hand end table is a [fine hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Hat "Skyrim:Fine Hat") and two gold coins. Higher up on the north wall is an easily-missed shelf with a silver ingot and medium coin purse, and a wash basin further to the right on a stand.

## Notes

- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the top right of the entrance door.
- The two unlocked chests do not respawn.

| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit%27s_Note_on_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure") |
| Location(s): | Svarig's camp (unmarked), [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave") |
| Reward: | [Nerveshatter](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter "Skyrim:Nerveshatter") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_MiscQuest\_Nerveshatter |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |

A fusion of [amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber "Skyrim:Amber") and [madness ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Madness Ore") is needed to find this hammer

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find more information on the bandits' mysterious leader.
2. Investigate [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave").
3. Place [amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber "Skyrim:Amber") and [madness ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Madness Ore") on the embers near [Gadnor](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor "Skyrim:Gadnor")'s body.
4. Retrieve Nerveshatter.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After reading [Svarig](/wiki/Skyrim:Svarig "Skyrim:Svarig")'s journal during the quest [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power"), you are given a miscellaneous quest to learn more about the gang's mysterious benefactor. Following the quest marker directs you to a camp east of Svarig's camp. Under one of the tents you'll find a knapsack containing the *[Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit%27s_Note_on_Hidden_Treasure "Skyrim:Bandit's Note on Hidden Treasure")*, which points you to [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave").

Upon entering the cave, you'll find the body of Gadnor on a stone bier, along with a small campsite. Next to the campsite is a makeshift altar to Kynareth, some minor loot, and the journal *[Gadnor's Last Wishes](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor%27s_Last_Wishes "Skyrim:Gadnor's Last Wishes")*. The journal explains that, according to his wishes, a friend of Gadnor placed him here and placed an illusion over his beloved warhammer Nerveshatter. In order to reveal the hammer, one must place 1x amber and 1x madness ore on the brazier near Gadnor's bier.

Doing so will reveal Nerveshatter and you can claim your prize. When you do so, Seducer bandits will show up and attack you.

## Notes

- Both amber and madness ore materials are rare, but you are guaranteed to find both if you did the quest [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order"). Within [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers") lies many hollowed tree stumps with a high chance to contain amber. On [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron")'s desk lies a piece of madness ore. Both items can be bought from [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad").
- After gaining Nerveshatter, you can take back the Amber and Madness Ore.
- Don't miss the Gadnor's Staff of Charming he holds on the rock and the Moonstone Ore Vein on the South wall half-way up the ramp.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_Nerveshatter stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_Nerveshatter`.

# Skyrim:New Allegiances

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image**. See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Vampires.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Vampires.png) | **Turn the target into a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Three [Potions of Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Blood "Skyrim:Potion of Blood") or an enchanted item, and access to a coffin in target's home |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1([Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran")), =1([Cairine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine")),  =1([Valindor](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor "Skyrim:Valindor")) |
| ID: | DLC1RV07 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:The Bloodstone Chalice") | | |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the specified location.
2. Turn the target into a vampire.
3. Report back to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo").

## Detailed Walkthrough

When asking what can be done to help around [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"), you may be directed to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo"). Speak to him, and he will tell you:

:   *"I've found a new candidate, ripe for Harkon's Gift. I'm sending you to welcome this soul into our family."*

Depending on who the target is, he will go on to say one of three things:

:   *"[Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") manages the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). A forsaken place under the shadow of the mages guild. She will help us keep an eye on the mages."*
:   *"[Valindor](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor "Skyrim:Valindor") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") has his ears in places that we'd love to listening in. Joining our family should increase our possibilities in the south."*
:   *"A [pathetic creature](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine") in her present condition, but the gift will embolden her. And her lowly state suits her to being our eyes and ears in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")."*

He then instructs you:

:   *Put her/his mind to rest, allay her/his fear through [vampiric seduction](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Seduction "Skyrim:Vampire's Seduction") and when she/he is in a pliant condition, embrace her/him and bite her/him on the neck."*

Additional questions on various subjects will be available before setting out:

:   **What do you mean by allaying fear through vampiric seduction?**

    :   *"Our blood grants us power to calm and relax. If you currently lack the gift, forgo feeding for a day and that power will come naturally.
        Once your thrall is suitable sedated, you will be able to impart the gift without resistance."*
:   **Can't anyone become a vampire if bitten by one?**

    :   *"While the blessed state of undeath can be 'accidentally' conferred - consider the brutish creatures you find wailing in dank hovels in the wild...
        Only those who can trace their ancestry through Harkon's mortal blood line*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *can faithfully accept the power conferred by his Vampiric blood.
        And among those, it seems, only when the heavens show the correct aspects.
        I have found such a soul and the stars appear cooperative."*
:   **Why am I able to bestow the gift of Harkon's blood?**

    :   *"Because he himself bestowed upon you a portion of his vitality when he infused you with his own blood the night you returned with Serana.
        A small measure of his blood now and forever flows through your veins."*
:   **Understood.**

    :   *"When you offer the embrace, do so away from prying eyes. Our new sibling will then likely require rest while his/her blood undergoes the change. Return to me when your part is done."*

In this quest you are required to infect either Haran, Valindor, or Cairine, earning their allegiance to the [Volkihar Vampire Clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan"). Vingalmo suggests that you use [Vampire's Seduction](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Seduction "Skyrim:Vampire's Seduction") to ease the process, but biting the target while they are asleep will also work.

### Valindor

[Valindor](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor "Skyrim:Valindor") can be found in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and starts off his day by waking up at 4am and having a long breakfast for two hours in his house. At 10pm, he returns to his house to sleep for six hours until 4am, and repeats his schedule the following day.

### Cairine

[Cairine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine") can be found in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and spends her entire day at the Warrens. She rarely sleeps, and instead sits on the ground, making her an easy target.

### Haran

[Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") can be found in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") at the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"). At 2am, she sleeps in the inn's cellar along with her daughter, [Eirid](/wiki/Skyrim:Eirid "Skyrim:Eirid").

Once you have bitten your target, they will be part of the Clan. Return to [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo") to complete the quest.

## Notes

- A coffin will be added to each new vampire's home, which you can then use to sleep and get the [vampire rested bonus](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Blood_Rested "Skyrim:Vampiric Blood Rested"). The new vampires do not seem to use it, however, and will still sleep in their old beds.
- Dialogue conditions in the game data suggest that it could have been possible for [Orthjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthjolf "Skyrim:Orthjolf") to give this quest, but he does not.
- If Vingalmo selects Valindor as the target, the door to Valindor's House will be locked if night falls while inside it. Unlocking the door will considered a crime. Just wait until 04:00 AM for the door to unlock itself.

## Bugs

- The quest giver may ask you to infect the same person if you have done this quest before. They cannot be turned into a vampire again.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Use the console command `setstage dlc1rv07 100` to move the quest to the next stage.
  - One fix to this bug is to kill the already infected vampire. It marks the quest as "failed" but still completes it.
  - Another fix is to load a previous save from before accepting the quest and try again, as they may not give the same quest.
  -  Finish any other active quests from the vampires, then go outside the castle and save. If any of the vampires send you to Vingalmo for work, reload the save, and, while outside, enter the `setstage DLC1RV07 255` in the console. This will complete the quest and give you the reward, and the questline will progress as usual.
  - After completing the quests for Vingalmo you can kill all targets and never receive the quest again.
- After biting the target your character may not be able to move, and you will not be able to complete the quest.
  - Reload from last autosave (should be from when you walk in) and feed from sneak mode.
- You may be unable to feed on Cairine (likely due to her sitting animation).
  -  One solution is to select her via the console (or by typing `prid D6702`) and enter the command `resurrect 1` which should force her to stand temporarily, or `moveto player` which should move her to you and force her to stand for longer. Once you close the console, immediately use your Vampire Seduction on her and rapidly press the activation/talk button, which should then allow you to access the feed option. Optionally, you may wish to toggle nearby Garvey's detection by selecting him in the console and typing `tdetect`.
  - To get Cairine to stand up, you can also punch her with your fists or use a weak spell in order to engage combat with her. Then you can just use Vampire Seduction.
- After your target becomes a vampire, they may never be tagged as undead, and gain access to no vampiric powers.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- After feeding on Cairine, the quest may not update and the quest marker will continue to point at her as if you have yet to feed.
- Vingalmo may not interact with you at all, even though everyone will keep telling you to speak to him.

# Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub

## Overview

New Gnisis Cornerclub

**New Gnisis Cornerclub** is a [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It is located in the Gray Quarter, next to [Sadri's Used Wares](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Used_Wares "Skyrim:Sadri's Used Wares").

The tavern is run by [Ambarys Rendar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ambarys_Rendar "Skyrim:Ambarys Rendar") and his employee, [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil"). Ambarys tends the counter while Malthyr cleans the taproom (he was supposed to take over the club if Ambarys dies, but doesn't, due to a [bug](#Bugs)). It consists of one area only, *[New Gnisis Cornerclub](#New_Gnisis_Cornerclub)*.

**NOTE**: Like all other stores, New Gnisis Cornerclub has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main trading room. These can be bought from the proprietors and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ambarys Rendar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ambarys_Rendar "Skyrim:Ambarys Rendar") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas") \*  [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") \*  [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") |

\* Depending on choices made during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest.

## Related Quests

Ground floor

- **[Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin")**: The [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") are after [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn"). Help him get to safety.
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## New Gnisis Cornerclub

The ground floor consists of the taproom, which is quite messy and worn-out. The front door opens to the sight of the bar, which seats four and has a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a wedge of [eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on display.

Hidden behind the bar is some [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). The shelves contain a bottle of Nord mead, two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). The only table for customers contains a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), and a bottle of Nord mead. To the north is the staircase leading to the second floor and, hidden underneath the stairs, sits the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*.

Second Floor

The second floor contains a number of items related to the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") Legion. Banners hang from the ceiling and an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") with matching [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield"), [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers"), [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots") can be found along the southern wall. The single table holds a loaf of bread, a boiled cream treat, and a bottle of alto wine.

The dresser holds lower-class [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and has a salt pile and the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")* on top. The wardrobe contains more clothes and the barrel contains food. The shelves hold a bottle of alto wine, a copy of *[The Firsthold Revolt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firsthold_Revolt "Skyrim:The Firsthold Revolt")* and the tavern's [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). Hidden underneath the stairs to the third floor is a rare bottle of [double-distilled skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Distilled_Skooma "Skyrim:Double-Distilled Skooma"), related to the quest [Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft").

Top floor

The top floor contains the owned bed where Malthyr Elenil sleeps between midnight and 8am. There is also an empty [pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Pot "Skyrim:Pot") and two large food sacks scattered on the floor. The table along the western wall contains the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a copy of *[The Arcturian Heresy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcturian_Heresy "Skyrim:The Arcturian Heresy")*, and a slice of bread. The two sets of shelves in the northwestern corner only contain a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a bottle of Nord mead, and some [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). A pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") is on the floor behind the bed, at the bottom of a dresser with clothes, which has a set of fixed [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") on top, along with twelve gold coins. At the foot of the table in the northeastern corner are three food sacks while the table itself holds a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and another food sack. Lastly is a table with a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") on top.

## Displayed Merchandise

- The following items are sitting out in the store on counters, shelves, or tables. They can be purchased or taken for free if your [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with Ambarys Rendar is high enough. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Food**: 1 [Boiled Creme Treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), 2 [Bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), 1 [Eidar Cheese Wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), 1 [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), 2 [Tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), 1 [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") - **Ingredients**: 1 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the cornerclub's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Rumors

- *"You didn't hear it from me, but if you want a real drink, head down to the New Gnisis Cornerclub, in the Gray Quarter."*
- *"The Dunmer get their drinks at the New Gnisis Cornerclub. Why they can't just call it a tavern is beyond me."*

## Notes

- The New Gnisis Cornerclub is likely a reference to [Gnisis](/wiki/Morrowind:Gnisis "Morrowind:Gnisis") in *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*.
- This is the only inn where you cannot rent a room.

## Bugs

- Malthyr is supposed to take over running the New Gnisis Cornerclub if Ambarys dies. Although he stands behind the bar as if he is running it, he does not offer any [services](/wiki/Skyrim:Services "Skyrim:Services").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- 3 of the cornerclub's regular customers ([Adelaisa Vendicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci"), [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya"), and [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye")) cannot use the furniture here due to the ownership of the bar stools and chairs being set to the WindhelmCornerclubPatrons faction which none of them are in, resulting in them standing around doing nothing when they're here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Ambrys sometimes welcomes you in by telling you that they have beds. This doesn't make sense given that there are no beds available for rent here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added to prevent that dialogue scene from playing in this particular location.

# Skyrim:Night Hunter

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Claim the belongings of a [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") vampire hunter.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading [Kragrash's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Kragrash%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Kragrash's Letter") |
| Location(s): | [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout"), [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") |
| Reward: | [Ebony Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Crossbow "Skyrim:Ebony Crossbow"), [Elven Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Elven Crossbow"), ability to craft them |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE043\_VampireHunterQuest |
| Added by: | [Elite Crossbows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows") |

A dead vampire hunter wishes to pass the torch to you

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout") and read *[Kragrash's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Kragrash%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Kragrash's Letter")*.
2. Locate Kragrash's burnt corpse on a cliff edge south of the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") and take his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar Key").
3. Return to Ironback Hideout and enter the [cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar") for your reward.

### Kragrash the Vampire Hunter

The quest starts when you read [Kragrash's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Kragrash%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Kragrash's Letter") at [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout"), a remote bandit camp high in the mountains of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"). This location can be quite difficult to reach as it only has one approach.

Defeat the [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") camped out at the hideout and locate *[Kragrash's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Kragrash%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Kragrash's Letter")* on the table inside the ruined house (it may be difficult to see). Searching the hideout, you may come across a new trapdoor beneath a tent. This trapdoor has been added by the Creation and is locked for now.

Claim Kragrash's crossbows for yourself

The letter reveals that Ironback Hideout used to be occupied by an [Orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") vampire hunter named Kragrash. He contracted [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") and subsequently became suicidal, hiking east into the mountains to watch one final sunrise before he turned. In his letter, he invites you to seek him out and claim his vampire hunting equipment.

You will need to travel to the nearby [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") to find Kragrash's final resting place. To the south of the embassy's entrance, you will come upon a burnt corpse on the edge of a cliff; this is the remains of Kragrash, who apparently covered himself in [Dwarven oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Oil "Skyrim:Dwarven Oil") and ensured that he would be burnt up in the sunlight. Loot his corpse to find the [Ironback Hideout Cellar Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar Key") which can be used on the trapdoor back at Ironback Hideout.

### Reward

With the key, you will have the ability to enter [Ironback Hideout Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar"), a remarkably well-preserved base of operations containing a vault filled with vampire hunting equipment. The quest will end once you enter the cellar and you'll gain the abilitiy to craft [Ebony Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Crossbow "Skyrim:Ebony Crossbow") and [Elven Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Elven Crossbow"), then you are free to unlock the vault and loot everything within. A Silver sword and greatsword can be found here. Laid out on a table you will find an [Ebony Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Crossbow "Skyrim:Ebony Crossbow"), an [Elven Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Elven Crossbow"), and several [Exploding Dwarven Bolts of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Fire "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Fire") and [Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Shock "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Shock"). These two powerful crossbows are the main reward for this quest, and can be enhanced using the nearby [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil").

## Notes

- The Enhanced variants for both crossbows can be crafted only and won't appear in merchant inventories similar to the expanded crossbows. The regular Ebony and Elven crossbows will be available for purchase from the [Fletcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Fletcher_(place) "Skyrim:Fletcher (place)") upon their discovery.
- This is one of the few locations, which is not added by the Dawnguard DLC, where Silver weaponry can be found without progressing through the Companions questline.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE043_VampireHunterQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE043_VampireHunterQuest`.

# Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Nightcaller Temple

**Nightcaller Temple** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") on the clifftop overlooking [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It contains only one zone, *[Nightcaller Temple](#Nightcaller_Temple)*.

Also known as the **Tower of Dawn** (see [notes](#Notes)), the temple is a ruin within a ruin. Originally a military fort that was later abandoned, it was subsequently occupied by [worshippers of Vaermina](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina_Devotee "Skyrim:Vaermina Devotee"). At some point after these Daedric devotees occupied the tower, an [Orc war party](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Invader "Skyrim:Orcish Invader") attacked, intending to destroy the [Skull of Corruption](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_of_Corruption "Skyrim:Skull of Corruption") which had inflicted them with terrible nightmares. Unable to fend off the Orcs, and in a last-ditch effort to protect the artifact, the worshippers released the Miasma, a gas that put everyone inside to sleep, and the temple fell into ruin once more.

Speaking to [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur"), a follower of Mara, in the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") will begin the quest [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") to end the locals' nightmares, which focuses on this location and its questionable past. Depending on your choices during the quest, Erandur may relocate to the ruin after its conclusion.

## Related Quests

- **[Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")**: Relieve the people of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") from [Vaermina](/wiki/Lore:Vaermina "Lore:Vaermina")'s curse.

### Exterior

Entrance

The entrance is guarded by three leveled [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures"). There are several [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes around the building. It is possible to climb the ruined wall to the right of the entrance, then jump on top of the ruined structure and proceed to the north side, where you will find an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Against the outer western wall of the building is a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein").

#### Shrine Chamber

Shrine of Mara

The entrance leads directly into the entry hall, where [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") has established a makeshift [shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") on the left-hand wall. A copy of *[Trials of St. Alessia](/wiki/Skyrim:Trials_of_St._Alessia "Skyrim:Trials of St. Alessia")* is on the table under the shrine. Prior to the start of the related quest, there are two [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in this room. A lectern at the back of the room holds three common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), with a novice-locked chest against the wall behind it. You are unable to explore past this first room until you start the related quest.

#### Inner Sanctum

There is a strange, almost mechanical noise coming from the back of the entrance hall, near the large central wall carving. After Erandur unlocks the carving during the related quest, it will become a shadowy curtain leading into the tower. In the middle of the tower lies the Skull of Corruption, a powerful [Daedric artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts") which feeds on the dreams of its victims. The ruins haven't been entered in a long time, judging from the dust and cobwebs. There are many crates and barrels found within the ruins, as well as many [Orcish invaders](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Invader "Skyrim:Orcish Invader") and [Vaermina devotees](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina_Devotee "Skyrim:Vaermina Devotee"). The number of invaders and devotees that revive depends on your level; any that do will be immediately hostile to both you and Erandur.

When you first enter with Erandur, he will lead you to the right until you can look through some grating down upon the Skull of Corruption. You can also see the magical barrier blocking access to the artifact and most of the ruins. Opposite the grating is a locked wooden door that requires a key to open. Descend the stairs as they curve around until you reach the barrier. There are two invaders at the bottom of the stairs, and a raised wooden grate blocking a passage to the northwest.

#### Library

After a brief conversation with Erandur, he will lead you back upstairs to the locked wooden door, which he will now unlock. Through the door is a short passage leading to the library, where you will find an invader and a devotee upstairs, and two more devotees and another invader downstairs. After any of these opponents that revive have been dealt with, Erandur will instruct you to find *[The Dreamstride](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dreamstride "Skyrim:The Dreamstride")*, a book that contains the information needed to pass the magical barrier. Most of the books in the library have been burnt and are worthless; however, in addition to the book you are looking for, the following can also be found: *[16 Accords of Madness, v. VI](/wiki/Skyrim:16_Accords_of_Madness,_v._VI "Skyrim:16 Accords of Madness, v. VI")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v2")*, *[Feyfolken II](/wiki/Skyrim:Feyfolken_II "Skyrim:Feyfolken II")*, *[On Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Oblivion "Skyrim:On Oblivion")*, *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*, *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, and *[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*. Downstairs, against the northeast wall, is a wooden door with an expert-locked chest behind it. Once you return to Erandur with the book, he will lead you along a passage to the northwest toward a laboratory, where he hopes to find a potion known as **[Vaermina's Torpor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina%27s_Torpor "Skyrim:Vaermina's Torpor")**. This concoction will enable you to enter the Dreamstride state and pass the magical barrier.

#### Laboratory

The passage leads into a storeroom that contains an invader and a devotee, as well as numerous unusable barrels, sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), and two sets of shelves holding a total of six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), nine bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and three [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). Against the northeast wall is a small shelving unit holding a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Beside this unit is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). On the floor are two large pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), a piece of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"), and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). In the western corner is a passage into the laboratory. Here you will find two devotees and an invader on the left, and a further devotee and invader on a lower level. Once they are taken care of, Erandur will explain what the Torpor potion looks like.

In this room are a total of three [alchemy labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), with three counters, two broken tables, one small round table, and many sets of shelves all the way around the lower part of the room. The items found in the room are:

1 [Blue Butterfly Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), 4 [Butterfly Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing"), 1 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), 1 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 2 [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"), 1 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 5 [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") (three hanging dried and two loose samples), 2 [Falmer Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), 3 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 2 [Frost Mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") (both hanging dried), 1 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") (hanging braid), 2 [Giant's Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), 1 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), 3 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 3 [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), 1 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), 4 [Luna Moth Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing"), 2 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), 4 [Nordic Barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), 1 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 1 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 4 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), 4 [Skeever Tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), 2 [Slaughterfish Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), 2 [Taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), 2 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), 4 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), 2 [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), 1 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts").

1 Random [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 2 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 2 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 3 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 4 [Potion of Resist Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Shock"), 1 [Vaermina's Torpor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina%27s_Torpor "Skyrim:Vaermina's Torpor").

7 [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), 1 [Carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), 1 [Dog Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), 1 [Horker Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), 2 [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), 6 [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

2 [Apothecary's Satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mannimarco, King of Worms](/wiki/Skyrim:Mannimarco,_King_of_Worms "Skyrim:Mannimarco, King of Worms")*, a copy of *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra").*

To the southeast from the lower level is a wide passage. On your immediate right, on the ground is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The passage leads to the wooden grate that was blocking access to/from the main passage next to the magical barrier. On the left is a handle that lowers it. Once you return to Erandur with the Torpor potion, he will instruct you to drink it.

#### Inner Sanctum Revisited

The barrier

Drinking the potion will cause you to enter the Dreamstride state, in which you will have to navigate the temple to re-enact the scene when the Miasma was originally released and the magical barrier was created. Once you have done this, you will be able to take the random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") that is maintaining the barrier, thus removing the barrier and allowing access to the rest of the ruin. You will then need to battle alongside Erandur back through the rooms and passages you traveled in the Dreamstride state in order to reach the Skull of Corruption. The path is completely linear, with more encounters with devotees and invaders as you proceed.

#### Passage to Sleeping Quarters

You will pass a raised alcove on your right that contains a wooden table, with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") built into it. On the table is a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a leveled [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and two random soul gems. Against the south wall is an unlocked chest. Shortly past this area, an alcove on the left has a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Next is a set of shelves on the right holding two bottles of wine and two empty wine bottles. The passage then turns north, and ends with a wooden door on your right.

#### Sleeping Quarters

The sleeping quarters

Through this door is a dormitory with four single unowned beds and two dressers, one of which has a set of [Vaermina robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina_Robes "Skyrim:Vaermina Robes") on top. Against the east wall is an unlocked chest. On the left, a flight of stairs leads down to nine more unowned single beds. Also in this area are two dressers containing a mix of common and [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), a cupboard containing clutter, another set of Vaermina robes and a pair of boots on the floor, and piles of food sacks in the corners. Beside the stairs is an adept-locked chest, with a long wooden table next to it holding a leveled potion of healing, a leveled potion of magicka, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small coin purse, and three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

To the west near the chest and table is a narrow passage leading to a dining room, which features five long wooden tables and benches holding a total of six bottles of alto wine. Around the room are several sets of shelves and sideboards holding another seven bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), two random potions of healing, and one random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). From here the passage continues to the north then west, passing on the left a small shelving unit holding two [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), two bottles of alto wine, and a bottle of Nord mead.

#### Inner Sanctum Finale

The inner sanctum

At the end, a wooden door opens into a room with a flight of stairs at the far end leading up to the Skull of Corruption. When you first enter, a cutscene will play where Erandur is greeted as "Brother Casimir" by two Vaermina devotees, [Veren Duleri](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") and [Thorek](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorek "Skyrim:Thorek") (the two devotees who were conversing at the start of your Dreamstride), revealing Erandur to be the person who initially released the Miasma and whose memory you used to travel past the magical barrier. Apart from the Skull of Corruption, the room contains an unlocked boss chest to the right of the platform where the staff is held, as well as two small shelving units holding two bottles of Nord mead among several empty wine bottles.

## Notes

- You cannot take a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") into the fort with you. If you are traveling with one, a notification on the screen will appear as soon as you enter; they will stand next to the entrance and wait until you exit. This includes anyone you summon via the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill.
- Due to the amount of Orc invaders and the randomization of the races for the devotees, Nightcaller Temple is a good location for collecting Orc and elven blood for [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane").
- Erandur claims that the temple was abandoned for decades before the devotees moved in. This implies that the temple may actually be the fort of Dawnstar that was destroyed in [2E 283](/wiki/Lore:Second_Era "Lore:Second Era").
- Each Vaermina Devotee has one leveled magicka potion and one random [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Each Orcish Invader has a small amount of gold and a piece of either [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") weaponry.
- Although the Miasma is supposed to degrade the minds of those exposed to its effects, Veren and Thorek don't appear to have been affected like everyone else.
- Based on many unused markers in the game files, it seems this location was originally known as **Syncope Sanctuary**. For example, an unused [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Syncope_Sanctuary_Key "Skyrim:Syncope Sanctuary Key") called **Syncope Sanctuary Key** can still be found in the game files, although it's unobtainable by normal means and doesn't actually open anything.
- Unused data for a location known as **Tower of Dawn** can also be found in the game files. This name is otherwise only used in a Dawnstar-specific [loading screen](/wiki/Skyrim:Loading_Screens "Skyrim:Loading Screens") which states: *"The Tower of Dawn sits on a mountain overlooking Dawnstar. It is rumored to be cursed."* Based on the unused data, it's possible "Tower of Dawn" was an earlier name for Nightcaller Temple, and the loading screen text was never updated. However, it's also possible the former is another name for the latter, and both names refer to the fort.
  - This is supported by Erandur's line while climbing the hill that "The tower on that hill is our destination. People around here call it "The Tower of the Dawn"

## Bugs

- If you sit on the slanted bench in the laboratory, your feet will clip into the floor. If you sit on the far right side of it, the slanted seat will clip through your armor as well. **?**
- If you sit on either bench in the hallway just after the room with the magical barrier, the camera will briefly show the Skull room directly behind them. Standing up from either bench will briefly yield the same results. **?**
- The enemies and containers outside of the dungeon may respawn despite it being classed as a "no reset zone". **?**

## Maps

- 

  Nightcaller Temple

Nightgate Inn

**Nightgate Inn** is an inn west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It contains two zones: *[Nightgate Inn](#Nightgate_Inn)* and *[Nightgate Inn Cellar](#Nightgate_Inn_Cellar)*.

[Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring") tends the counter, buying and selling [food and drinks](#Standard_Merchandise), and renting out rooms for 10 gold.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim")  [Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") |

#### Creation Club

- **[Brothers in Irons](/wiki/Skyrim:Brothers_in_Irons "Skyrim:Brothers in Irons")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Iron "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Iron"): Investigate a wanted criminal.

#### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.

#### Imperial Legion

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)")**: Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

### Nightgate Inn

Inside Nightgate Inn

The room for rent

Like many other taverns, Nightgate Inn consists of a huge taproom with a fireplace in the center and the counter at the opposite end of the room from the entrance. Three wooden tables are scattered around the taproom, all of them set with food and drink. In addition to the taproom, the inn also has three smaller rooms with single beds, one of them reserved for paying customers, and a set of stairs leading down to the basement.

To the left when you enter, is the first table which is dressed with two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and one bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). In the northeastern corner stands three food barrels. Next to the barrels are another table with two loaves of bread, and more wine and alto wine, two bottles of each. The next table is where you can usually find permanent resident [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim"). The table in front of him is dressed with three loaves of bread, two bottles of alto wine, and one bottle of regular wine. Next up is a set of shelves with two [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). The bar takes up most of the northwestern part of the taproom and [Hadring](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadring "Skyrim:Hadring") can be found behind the counter 24 hours a day. On display is a wedge, a slice, and a wheel of eidar cheese, and the same of goat cheese, excluding the wheel. A bottle of wine and a bottle of alto wine are also on display. Hidden on the shelves underneath the counter are five gold coins, a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), three [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), fourteen bottles of Nord mead, six bottles of wine, two bottles of alto wine, and a copy of the book *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*. In the southern corner is a set of shelves with two bottles of alto wine and six of regular wine, along with four loaves of bread. Next to the shelves are two food barrels. Hanging from the ceiling, above the stairs leading down into the basement, are six dead [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Hanging next to the game are a few ingredients, including two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), some [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam").

The room you can rent is the first room along the southern wall and contains a single bed, a wardrobe with random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), a chest with minor loot at the foot of the bed, and a copy of *[Walking the World, vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, along with a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). The neighboring room can be used by the courier in the Imperial version of [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)"). It contains a dresser with clothes, several common books, and a chest with some loot. Opposite these two rooms is another room, which is larger and has a double bed owned by Hadring. Several books are stacked on two dressers with clothes, that also have a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and three bottles of Nord mead on top. Hidden in the northern corner, behind three food sacks, is a coin purse. Along the eastern wall sits an empty chest and in the northwestern corner are two bottles of alto wine.

### Nightgate Inn Cellar

[Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob")'s room

Down the stairs from the taproom is the cellar where mysterious Orc resident [Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") resides. It consists of a huge storage area and a smaller room for Balagog. The storage area has numerous inactive beer kegs and crates, along with six food barrels and six food sacks. In the northeastern corner is an exit to Skyrim.

Balagog's room contains a double bed with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") at the foot, a wardrobe with clothes, two end tables with clutter, and four food sacks. In the southwestern corner is a small table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on top. The end table to the northwest has a bottle of alto wine on top, with another bottle lying on the floor. The end table to the northeast has a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top, right next to a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[Legend of Krately House](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House")*.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Hadring's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- If you kill Balagog outside during Recipe for Disaster and drag him into the pond, the water will turn red, as if tainted with blood.
- Unused keys and merchant chests indicate the inn was intended to be part of a village known as **Heljarchen**, which previously appeared in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Places "Arena:Places")* as [Helarchen Creek](/wiki/Arena:Helarchen_Creek "Arena:Helarchen Creek").
  - There are unused keys for two farmhouses, one belonging to **Heigen**, and the other to **Jens**. It's possible these people lived with other additional NPCs.
  - Two other keys refer to normal houses, one under the name of **Fathendas**, and the other under **Traillus**. Two unused merchant chests also exist, one for an apothecary and one for a blacksmith, but it's unknown which NPCs owned these chests. The blacksmith chest can still be found in the final game, underneath the map.
  - Two fishing markers placed nearby name two more NPCs, **Belayn** and **Felisi**, who might have been local fishermen (or women), but nothing more is known about them.
  - The [Griefstricken Chef](/wiki/Skyrim:Griefstricken_Chef "Skyrim:Griefstricken Chef") is internally known as `DBRecurringContact9Heljarchen`, suggesting he was originally intended to appear in the village, rather than in Dawnstar where he appears in the final game.
  - The name of the village was later reused for [the constructable house](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") added by [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire").
  - One line spoken by Balagog gro-Nolob still refers to "the village", one of the only references to the planned location remaining in the game.
- Two [orichalcum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") veins are 300 feet south of the inn.
- If Dawnguard is installed, a Dawnguard Cache can be found at the base of the pier after locating [Saliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Saliah "Skyrim:Saliah").
- If Hearthfire is installed, three [clay](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") deposits can be found east of the inn on the bank of the pond.
- If Hearthfire is installed, you won't be able to tell your carriage driver at your house to take you here.
-  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels and harvestable salmon outside as owned by the inn.

# Skyrim:Nightingale Hall

## Overview

The entrance to Nightingale Hall

**Nightingale Hall** is the home of the [Nightingales](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales") between Riften and [the Shadow Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shadow_Stone "Skyrim:The Shadow Stone").

Blocked entrance early in the game

## Related Quests

- **[Trinity Restored](/wiki/Skyrim:Trinity_Restored "Skyrim:Trinity Restored")**: Become one of the Nightingales, [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal")'s guardians.

## Nightingale Hall

The entrance to Nightingale Hall is a rather steep and narrow incline, illuminated by fissures in the ceiling and decorated with Nightingale sigil banners. The narrow trail opens to the hall: an impressive cavern, complete with waterfall and rushing stream. Crossing the wooden bridge spanning the stream, you will reach the living quarters. After the Hall is restored (see [notes](#Notes)), a small round table will hold [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a piece of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), a wedge of [Eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a piece of bread, and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). A bookshelf will hold some reading material, and an unlocked chest at the foot of the nearby bed will contain some gold. The next bed over will have an end table with a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Purloined Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Purloined_Shadows "Skyrim:Purloined Shadows")* on top (before the Hall's restoration, the book will be on the ground).

The next room is the circular armory with the three [Nightingale Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Armor "Skyrim:Nightingale Armor") pedestals involved in the related quest. The hallway continues southward, with branches to the east and west. Taking the east passage, to the left, brings you to an unused training room with discarded practice dummies. On the south wall is a novice-locked chest. The passage to the west leads to an additional bedroom, with two beds and a bedroll. A copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")* is next to the bed on the left, and between the two beds is a novice-locked chest.

Continuing to the south, you come to the Oath room, with the three platforms representing the Trinity. While this room is a quiet place for reflection, it holds nothing of note.

## Notes

- Before [Trinity Restored](/wiki/Skyrim:Trinity_Restored "Skyrim:Trinity Restored"), the entrance is blocked.
- There are two  "Safe") Safe [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") on birch tree stumps outside Nightingale Hall.
- Although Karliah says she will, she may not live in or visit the Hall until you [finish](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_New_Management "Skyrim:Under New Management") restoring the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to its former glory and become the Guild Master. She will then attend your ceremony and return to Nightingale Hall, which will now be restored and upgraded.[*verification needed*]

## Bugs

- Nightingale Hall does not have [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") set as a parent location.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.

## Gallery
