# Skyrim:Nilheim

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Tower.png) | Nordic Tower: Nilheim ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| NilheimExterior01, NilheimExterior02, NilheimExterior03 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| East-northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") Northwest of [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Nilheim

**Nilheim** is a small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east-northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") disguised as guards.

## Related Quests

- **[Telrav's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav%27s_Request "Skyrim:Telrav's Request")**: Escort [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav") back to his camp in Nilheim.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Nilheim's deceit

If you do not first speak to [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav"), the occupants are disguised as [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_(NPC) "Skyrim:Guard (NPC)") and are non-hostile. You can loot everything in the tower without any of them caring.

If you do speak to Telrav and initiate his [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav%27s_Request "Skyrim:Telrav's Request") to return him to his camp, all of these "friendly" guards are revealed to be [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Killing Telrav unprovoked without initiating the quest results in the guards being hostile when you approach. After speaking to Telrav, he will lead you across the bridge and up several flights of stairs until you reach the main camp. At this point he will reveal his true colors and attack along with the bandits in the main camp. Once they are dealt with there may still be one of the imitation guards on the second floor of the tower. He will be hostile when you approach.

Nilheim camp

The main camp consists of a campfire with three long wooden tables and benches arranged around it. One of these has a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a sack of food on top, the next has an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside it, and the third has two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") and two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") on top and three food barrels beside it with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on one of these. To the north of the fire is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").

More stairs rise to the southwest; at the top is a ruined wall and to the right of this is a stone bridge crossing to the tower. Inside, there is a dresser opposite the door with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on top. Stairs lead from here to a wooden ramp that takes you up to the next floor, where you may find a hostile imitation guard. There is a table next to the entrance with a leveled war axe, a large coin purse, an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a leveled [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency") on top and several food sacks underneath. Farther into the room are three unowned bedrolls around an extinguished fire and several barrels and sacks of food. There are wooden stairs up with a wardrobe underneath.

The top of the tower has an unlocked chest as well as an awe-inspiring view of southeast [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). On a clear day, one can see the entire [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains") that surround southeastern Skyrim, and to the north one can see farther than [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). To the west the view is blocked by the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"), and [Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit") to the east.

There are two unnamed bodies, an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)") and a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)"), thrown among the rocks at the base of the tower to the north. Farther down the slope on the rock cliff is the body of a bandit.

## Notes

- Though the bandits are named after the standard "Bandit", they'll be stronger than the usual bandits, but won't level and be named (for example, "Bandit Marauder", "Bandit Thug").
- There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") a few paces to the south of the south end of the bridge to the tower. With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, a [clay desposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") can be found south of there.
- A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") can be found underneath the eastern end of the main bridge that leads to the dungeon.

## Bugs

- When the bandits are disguised as guards, they may not be hostile even if you approach as a werewolf.
- When the bandits are disguised as guards, they are only friendly toward you, but not toward your [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") or [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). They will attack and even kill your horse if you ride it to Nilheim.
- If a radiant quest sends you here after you have cleared the tower, it will be impossible to complete.
  - Reload a previous save and obtain a different location for the quest.
  - Alternatively, enter the following commands in the console to resurrect the bandit chief of the tower and teleport him to you: `prid 72a8d`, `resurrect` and then `moveto player`.
- If you attack Telrav to make him hostile before the quest marker, but don't kill him, the guards will only watch and Telrav will not attack you.
- The items and containers may respawn despite Nilheim being classed as a "no reset zone". **?**

# Skyrim:Nimhe, the Poisoned One

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill the giant frostbite spider blocking access to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Access to the Dwemer Museum and [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo")) |
| ID: | FreeformMarkarthO |
| Suggested Level: | 16 |

Nimhe blocking the entrance to Nchuand-Zel

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to Calcelmo in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep").
2. Kill [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe"), a giant [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").

### The Scholar

Calcelmo, an accomplished scholar and author, is the owner and curator of the private [Dwemer museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") and the associated [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel#Nchuand-Zel_Excavation_Site "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel") archaeological dig site. Should you wish to enter either of these locales, you must go through Calcelmo. He spends his time at the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") set up across the underground river from the entrance to the Nchuand-Zel excavation site. Talk to him about his work, and he will inform you that he has been placed in charge of curating artifacts extracted from Nchuand-Zel, an ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") castle located deep within the mountain behind Understone Keep. He mentions his excavation efforts being thwarted by the presence of Nimhe, a giant frostbite spider that is blocking the entrance to Nchuand-Zel. He asks you to kill the spider in exchange for access to both his Dwemer museum and the site itself. If you agree, he will give you the [key to Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Key to Nchuand-Zel").

### Nchuand-Zel

The entrance to the Nchuand-Zel excavation site is a large metal door at the top of a short flight of stairs directly across the stone bridge from where Calcelmo's arcane enchanter is set up. Once inside, you will encounter a set of two square rooms connected to each other, with staircases on all sides of each room. All staircases are blocked by crumbled stone except the one at the far left, which provides access to the excavation site. After proceeding through a short passage, you will descend into an area which is still under excavation (mostly dirt and wooden scaffolding), and encounter two or three frostbite spiders. After killing these, you will proceed a little deeper into the excavation area, where you will come across a seemingly dead end, with webs on part of the wall. Look closely and you will see that some of the webbing is blocking a passage. Cut through the webs to provide access to the passage, which leads to a room with a raised stone walkway with stairs at the opposite end, covered with spider webs. If you look up, you will see the large webbed hole in the ceiling through which Nimhe will descend once you approach.

### Cleaning House

Dispatching of Nimhe may prove difficult within the tight quarters, since there is very little room to maneuver in order to pull back from her attacks. An option is to retreat back down the corridor from which you came and attack Nimhe with ranged weapons or spells, as she cannot fit in the passage. Once the deed is done, search through more webbing at the top of the stone walkway to find the body of [Alethius](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius "Skyrim:Alethius"), and clues leading to [another quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition") within Nchuand-Zel.

Once you inform Calcelmo of the giant spider's demise he will award you the [Dwemer Museum key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key"), allowing access at any time. Following the completion of this quest, the various Dwemer metal parts on the two tables near Calcelmo and his nephew may now be taken without consequence.

## Notes

- Despite access to Nchuand-Zel being promised by Calcelmo as a reward for this quest, the area may be accessed, and thus Nimhe encountered, beforehand by picking the lock on the excavation site door.
- You can access Nchuand-Zel without killing Nimhe, but this may prove rather difficult, as her large body blocks a good deal of the rather small antechamber preceding the entrance.
- This quest can be done in conjunction with the quests "[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")" and "[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer")" to allow legal entry to the Dwemer Museum but not to [Calcelmo's Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo%27s_Laboratory "Skyrim:Calcelmo's Laboratory"), further beyond.

## Bugs

- Nimhe may respawn upon returning to the Nchuand-Zel Excavation Site after a long enough period of time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Nimhe, the Poisoned One (FreeformMarkarthO) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Kill Nimhe inside Nchuand-Zel |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Tell Calcelmo that Nimhe is dead |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformMarkarthO stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformMarkarthO`.

# Skyrim:Niranye's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Niranye's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Niranye%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |

| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |

| Special Features | |

Niranye's House in Windhelm

**Niranye's House** is a residence in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

It is a large single-story house immediately to the east of the main gates into [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), with the rear of the house formed by part of the walls that surround the city. It has a yard between the side entrance and [Calixto's House of Curiosities](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_House_of_Curiosities "Skyrim:Calixto's House of Curiosities"), with a barrel in the northeastern corner (see [notes](#Notes)) and a wooden bench.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Fence") |

## Related Quests

- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")**: Remove a rival guild from the picture.

## Niranye's House

Niranye's house

There are two entrances: a front entrance, and a side entrance which is in the yard attached to the property. The house is locked with novice-level locks on both doors whenever Niranye is not present and at night. When entering through the front door, you enter into the middle of three rooms, containing end tables on either side of the door, a dresser opposite against the south wall with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top, and a fancy [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on the floor to the left. Against the east wall, to the right of a doorway, is a set of shelves holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), and a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). Against the west wall is a column of three wall shelves with a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") on them (see [bugs](#Bugs)). There is a chair in the southwestern corner, and another to the right of a doorway on the west wall.

The doorway leads into Niranye's bedroom, which contains an owned double bed coming out from the west wall, an end table in the southwestern corner, and a set of shelves against the south wall holding several sets of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and copies of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[The Firsthold Revolt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firsthold_Revolt "Skyrim:The Firsthold Revolt")*, with a wash basin on a stand to the right of the shelves. Against the north wall is a dresser containing more clothes, and against the east wall is a cupboard holding a bottle of alto wine and four more common books. The doorway to the east leads into the kitchen and dining room, with an entrance on the east wall and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks all around the room. There is a wooden table with two chairs in the middle of the room, with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a bowl containing two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top. In the southeastern corner is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, with a pile of firewood beside it. There are a couple cauldrons in the southwest corner. Against the north wall is a set of shelves holding a bottle of Nord mead, a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a wooden bowl containing four bunches of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and a cast iron pot containing two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), with a basket containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") to the right. Against the west wall, to the right of the doorway to the middle room, is a cupboard holding a bowl of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), and a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"). There is a hidden panel in the south wall between the cauldrons and the cooking pot, behind which is a flight of wooden stairs leading down to the right. At the bottom is a master-locked door that opens into Niranye's basement.

## Niranye's Basement

Niranye's basement

The basement consists of one large dimly lit room with a practice dummy in the southwestern corner, a small unit and a tall wardrobe against the west wall, a small square wooden table and two chairs, a set of shelves, and an expert-locked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") against the north wall, and a couple food barrels with a crate in front and two archery dummies on either side against the east wall. Everything is empty except for the safe, which contains some average loot along with two letters from [Linwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Linwe "Skyrim:Linwe") which relate to the [reputation quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows"), but aren't vital to the quest's successful completion.

## Notes

- This barrel only appears once you have completed the relevant [reputation quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows"). It is marked with the  "Cache") Cache Shadowmark, and is one of three thieves' caches found in the city.
- The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pit_Key "Skyrim:Darkwater Pit Key") to the safe in the concealed basement can be obtained by [pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") Niranye (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Bugs

- Niranye's safe key is incorrectly named the [Darkwater Pit Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pit_Key "Skyrim:Darkwater Pit Key").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- You can't interact with the goat hide.

# Skyrim:No Contest

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Take part in a fishing contest.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") |
| Location(s): | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") |
| Reward: | [Warlock's Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Warlock's Ring") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Morthal |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Heart of Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Gold "Skyrim:Heart of Gold") | **Next →** [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Heart of Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Gold "Skyrim:Heart of Gold") | | → Next | [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | | |

Face the fishing challenge issued by Brutius of Morthal

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") and read the [contest notice](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice:_Fishing_Contest "Skyrim:Notice: Fishing Contest").
2. Travel to [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and make a wager with [Brutius](/wiki/Skyrim:Brutius "Skyrim:Brutius").
3. Locate the fishing spot east of Morthal.
4. Defend yourself.
5. Read *[Brutius's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Brutius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Brutius's Journal")* and fish up the [Warlock's Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Warlock's Ring").

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can be started after [Heart of Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Gold "Skyrim:Heart of Gold") has been completed by talking to Viriya:

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"You're headed to Morthal. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [notice](/wiki/Skyrim:Notice:_Fishing_Contest "Skyrim:Notice: Fishing Contest") about a fishing contest in Morthal. Read it and then head to Morthal to meet up with [Brutius](/wiki/Skyrim:Brutius "Skyrim:Brutius"), speak to him:

:   **I'm here for the fishing contest. Are you ready to begin?**
:   *"Yeah."*
:   **You're Brutius? I expected someone younger. You're just a feeble old man.**
:   *"I don't have to take that from you!"*
:   **Shall we make a wager, then?**
:   *"How much?"*

    :   **100 gold.**
    :   **500 gold.**
    :   **1000 gold!**
    :   *"A little coin always greases the wheels."*
:   **Where shall we hold the contest?**
:   *"Here's where you need to go."*

The fishing spot

The fishing spot with [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") installed

The fishing contest spot is east of Morthal and will be marked on your map. When you arrive you will find out the contest is a trap, with Brutius and two bandits ambushing you. You may have to wait a little while for them to arrive. Brutius and the two bandits are all mages and will use magic attacks against you.

Once you have dispatched of the ambushers, loot the bandits who both have a full set of vagrant robes on and then search Brutius for his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Brutius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Brutius's Journal"). The journal tells of how Brutius has been leading other victims to the same ambush and how he dropped his ring in the river. Look for the fishing supplies by the river to fish for the ring. If you don't have a rod, Brutius has one on his body. Eventually you will fish up the [Warlock's Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Warlock's Ring"), ending the quest.

## Notes

- The fishing spot for this quest is just across the river from [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch_(place) "Skyrim:Myrwatch (place)"), added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). This Creation previously [made mention](/wiki/Lore:Anora%27s_Journal_(old) "Lore:Anora's Journal (old)") of the Warlock's Ring, but this reference was removed soon after its release. It can therefore be assumed that the tower being fully in frame when you retrieve the ring during this quest is not coincidental.

## Bugs

- If Brutius or one of the bandits is raised before the rest are killed, the quest will be stuck at this stage and Brutius's journal will not be present on his body, no matter if you kill the ambusher after they have been raised. This may occur due a follower like [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") who often raises fallen enemies in battle. **?**
  - If this bug occurs due to your follower, reload a previous save and tell them to wait somewhere far away from the battle, so they will not join the fight and you will be able to advance the quest.
- Brutius may have 2 journals; taking both will make it impossible to read the book to progress. **?**
  -  This can be fixed using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `help Brutius` to get the [FormID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") of the book, followed by `player.drop <FormID> 1`. The remaining book will then be readable.
- The contest notice remains marked as a quest item after the quest ends.
  -  Use the console command `player.removeitem xx000B2E 1` to remove the item from your inventory.

## Quest Stages

| No Contest (ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Morthal) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | A fisherman named Brutius is challenging anyone who would face him to a fishing contest. He requires his challengers to make a wager on who the better fisher is. If I want to test my fishing abilities against him, I should meet him on the docks in Morthal. *Objective 0:* Talk to Brutius in Morthal about a fishing contest |
| 10 |  | I placed a bet with Brutius that I could best him in a fishing contest. He marked where we will have the contest on my map. I should meet him there when I am ready to face him. *Objective 10:* Meet Brutius at the fishing spot |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Defeat Brutius |
| 20 |  | It seems that the fishing contest was nothing more than a trap. Brutius and several other wizards ambushed me as soon as I arrived at the location for the fishing contest. I will have to defeat them before I can find any answers. *Objective 20:* Defeat the ambushers |
| 30 |  | I defeated Brutius and the rest of his ambushers. I should search him to see if he kept a journal of his misdeeds. *Objective 30:* Search Brutius |
| 30 |  | I defeated Brutius, who turned out to be a wizard disguised as a fisherman. I wonder what other secrets he might have been keeping. I should search him to see if he kept a journal. *Objective 30:* Search Brutius |
| 40 |  | On Brutius's body, I found a journal. I should read it to discover what secrets he's been keeping. *Objective 40:* Read Brutius's journal |
| 50 |  | It seems that Brutius was a wizard that has been luring unsuspecting fisherman into the woods under the guise of a fishing contest, only to slay and rob them. Of note is an enchanted ring that he recently lost in the river at the fishing spot he lured his victims. I might be able to claim it if I try fishing there myself. *Objective 50:* Fish up Brutius's lost ring |
| 200 | ☑ | Tamriel is a better place without Brutius preying upon the citizens of Morthal. I also managed to fish up the Warlock's Ring, the ring Bruitus *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* lost at the spot near the river where he lured his victims. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 32, 35.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Morthal stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Morthal`.

# Skyrim:No News is Good News

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find out about the fate of [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard")'s daughter from [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") |
| Location(s): | [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics"), [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") |
| Reward: | None |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard")) |
| ID: | SolitudeFreeform01 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

*"Have you been to Whiterun?"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") in [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics").
2. Get some news from [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis").
3. Return to Angeline Morrard.

### A Mother's Request

[Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") is the shopkeeper of [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). In your conversation with her, she will ask you if you have been to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). If you tell her that you haven't been there before, she will be understanding and you can talk to her about it later. If you tell her that you have indeed been to Whiterun, she will become very animated. It seems her daughter, Fura, was assigned to Whiterun after she joined the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and Angeline was hoping to get some recent news about her. Although Angeline has tried contacting [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis"), she didn't get any information from him. If you are willing to help her get more information about her daughter, anything you can find out would be welcome.

### A Need To Know Basis

Captain Aldis can be found training the guards in the courtyard of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") during the day. When you tell him that Angeline sent you for information about her daughter, Aldis will respond, *"Generally posting information is need to know only"*. Several options are available for you to continue the conversation, including persuasion and intimidation. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him to reveal Fura's fate.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I think Angela *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* needs to know. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: I... I've been trying to find the time and place to let her know. **Failed**: I'm sorry, I can't help you. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Angeline **Failed**: Nothing |
| Well, I'm making it "need to know." **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: If you want to know that bad then fine. **Failed**: I'm afraid that kind of thing doesn't work on Captains in the Imperial Army. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Angeline **Failed**: Nothing |
| Fine. If that's the way you want it. | That's the way it is. | | | | Nothing |
| Tell me about her daughter. That's an order, Captain. | Yes, Sir. Although I'm not sure you'll be happy to know. | | | | Return to Angeline |

### The Casualty List

*"She needs to be told."*

The captain will then give you the news: *"Her daughter was sent to Whiterun, the skirmishes there have been violent. The whiterun*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *legate, he needed to know the Stormcloak positions. He sent out a party to scout the area. They happened upon a large force... I'm told none of them made it back. Private Morrard... Angela's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *daughter was in that scouting party. She needs to be told"*.

### The Bearer of Bad News

Return to Angeline Morrard with the news. Angeline is eager to hear about her daughter. She is understandably grief-stricken when you tell her the bad news: *"I told her. I told her the imperial*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *army would kill her. That this was a war of Jarls and Imperial Generals and we had no part in it. She just wouldn't hear it"*. Angeline can't thank you for the news, *"not for this"*, but she acknowledges that you have done her a service. You get no reward from her, but she will have a more friendly [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you and allow you to freely take many low-value items in her shop.

## Bugs

- If you have already accepted this quest before speaking with [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") he will not offer his favor quest, [Delivery (Sorex)](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Sorex) "Skyrim:Delivery (Sorex)").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- If you have completed the Stormcloak missions, especially [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), before speaking with Aldis, this quest will be impossible to finish as it would lead you to a bare area where Aldis once stood. Because of this, it is highly recommended this quest is done before finishing the Stormcloak missions.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - This can also be fixed by entering the following in the console: `setstage SolitudeFreeform01 20`. This will set the stage of the quest to where you have to return to Angeline, and will allow you to complete the quest.
- Captain Aldis will incorrectly refer to female characters as "sir" when he is asked about Angeline's daughter.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You can order Captain Aldis to give you the information even if you're not of the proper rank in the Imperial Legion, or if you're not a member of the Legion at all.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- You can exit the dialogue with Captain Aldis right after Persuade/Intimidate check before advancing quest stage. Therefore it can be repeated for leveling Speech up.

## Quest Stages

| No News is Good News (SolitudeFreeform01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Ask Aldis for information about Angeline's daughter. |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Tell Angeline what Aldis said. |
| 30 |  | *(Completes quest successfully)* |
| 200 | ☑ | *(Fails quest if stage 30 not complete)* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage SolitudeFreeform01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest SolitudeFreeform01`.

# Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic after completing [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") and going to jail |
| Location(s): | [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") |
| Reward: | [Shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv "Skyrim:Shiv"), [Silver-Blood Family Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Family_Ring "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Family Ring") and/or [Armor of the Old Gods](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_of_the_Old_Gods "Skyrim:Armor of the Old Gods") (see [notes](#Notes)) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Thonar Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood")) if Madanach killed |
| ID: | MS02 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") | | |

The prison cell in which you awaken at the beginning of the quest

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Complete [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") and go to jail.
2. Brawl, bribe, and/or lie your way into a meeting with [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach").
3. Follow Madanach's instructions and escape with the rest of the prisoners, *or* kill Madanach and escape on your own.

### Doing Time

Borkul the Beast

You will arrive in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") after completing the quest [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") and choosing to go to jail, where [Urzoga gra-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzoga_gra-Shugurz "Skyrim:Urzoga gra-Shugurz") tells you that you will have to mine for your freedom. Your journal will inform you that you must find [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach"), also known as the King in Rags, to help clear your name. Head through the gate, walk down the wooden platform, and talk to miner [Uraccen](/wiki/Skyrim:Uraccen "Skyrim:Uraccen") who is sitting by the fire.

Uraccen will say that you won't be able to speak with Madanach unless you can get past his bodyguard [Borkul the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Borkul_the_Beast "Skyrim:Borkul the Beast"). Uraccen can entertain you with a story of one of Borkul's exploits before you go speak with him. Borkul is guarding one of the three gates in this room. When you ask him to see Madanach, he tells you that the toll for entry is a [shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv "Skyrim:Shiv"). As alternatives to his request, you can brawl with him, intimidate or persuade him, or pickpocket the key from him.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I don't have a shiv. | Then find one. That dung heap Grisvar's been known to make a few. | | | | Find a shiv |
| Here's your shiv. | All right, head on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach is smarter than you think. | | | | Pass the door |
| Madanach is expecting me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Hmph. Fine. Go on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach knows more than you think. **Failed**: The only thing Madanach expects is a bottle of Skooma in tribute every so often. You're not getting through. | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door **Failed**: Nothing |
| How about some skooma instead? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Ah, now that's a good idea. Head on in. But don't try anything in there. Madanach is smarter than you think. | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door |
| Let me through, pig-face. **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Those eyes. All right, killer, go on through. But don't try anything. Madanach knows more than you think. **Failed**: That's what I was hoping you'd say. | | | | **Passed**: Pass the door **Failed**: Turn hostile |
| How about I fight you for it? **(Brawl)** | **Brawl**: That's what I was hoping you'd say.  - **Victory**: It's been so long since I tasted my own blood. Sour.   - **You'll let me through now?**   - Yeah, yeah. Go on in. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | | | | Brawl |
| I'll pay the toll later. | That's right. Turn around and leave. | | | | Nothing |

To get a shiv, talk to [Grisvar the Unlucky](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky"), who will ask for a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). To get the skooma, you have to find [Duach](/wiki/Skyrim:Duach "Skyrim:Duach") and pass a speech challenge, win a brawl, or pickpocket him.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I need some. Badly. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Getting the shakes, huh? All right. Take it. Old gods keep you. **Failed**: Skooma addict. Get lost. | | | | **Passed**: Get the skooma **Failed**: Nothing |
| Hand over the skooma. **(Brawl)** | **Passed**: Easy there. I didn't mean nothing. Take it.  **Brawl**: That's it.  - **Victory**: Damn addicts always stealing from me.   - **Now give me that skooma.**   - Here. I hope you choke on it. - **Failure**: (Nothing) | | | | **Passed**: Get the skooma **Failed**: Brawl |
| Never mind. | Smart. | | | | Nothing |

Bring the skooma to Grisvar, who will give you the shiv. If you want to keep the shiv, then you can still attempt the alternatives to completing Borkul's request. You can pickpocket an additional bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") from [Duach](/wiki/Skyrim:Duach "Skyrim:Duach") and bribe Borkul with it. Alternately, you can also start a battle with the Forsworn prisoners (attack anyone but Grisvar). This locks you into killing Madanach, as he becomes hostile. This fight can be difficult; you have no armor, no enchantments, and your only non-conjured weapons are pickaxes and possibly shivs, though you can still use any magic or powers that you may possess. Once you've won, loot the key off Borkul's body and proceed to kill Madanach per the next section.

### The King in Rags

Planning to escape

Once you get past the Orc, you will see Madanach sitting at a desk. He will direct some disparaging remarks at you regarding your predicament, and ask you what you want. Here, you can take one of two paths: take your revenge, or find your answers. If you seek revenge, you can kill Madanach here (or at any time) and then escape on your own. If you want a fair fight, you can tell him you plan to kill him; otherwise, just attack him. Attacking him will make all of the other prisoners hostile (except Grisvar), but as long as they are out of range, they will not rush in to join the fight. Search Madanach's body for a key and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach%27s_Note "Skyrim:Madanach's Note"), then unlock the gate and exit the prison.

If you seek answers instead, Madanach will direct you to [Braig](/wiki/Skyrim:Braig "Skyrim:Braig"), another prisoner, to hear his story of injustice. After you have convinced Braig to tell his story, return to Madanach. You will see a different side of Madanach, and the horrors that drive his purpose. He tells you he wants to return to the war and will help you escape as well, but only if you prove your loyalty to him by killing Grisvar the Unlucky. If you gave your shiv to Borkul, you can get a new one from Madanach at this point. Find Grisvar and kill him. If you tell him that, *"Madanach says hello"*, Grisvar will eventually become hostile and the other inmates will attack him. Once he's dead, return to Madanach, who will declare you an honorary member of the Forsworn and lead the prisoners to the escape tunnel.

### Escape

Fighting for freedom

After a short speech, follow Madanach and the Forsworn through the tunnel to [Markarth Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Ruins "Skyrim:Markarth Ruins"). You will encounter a pair of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), then one or two [Dwarven Spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") as you make your way through the ruins. If you're on your own, you can sneak off the bridge onto the floor below, as fighting alone will be quite difficult without any of your normal equipment. Once past the automatons, continue through the ruins until you reach a short tunnel that leads to a door to Markarth. Thonar will return your equipment and give you the [Silver-Blood Family Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Family_Ring "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Family Ring") if you are on your own and have killed Madanach when you exit the gates.

If you sided with Madanach, a Forsworn woman named [Kaie](/wiki/Skyrim:Kaie "Skyrim:Kaie") will be there to return your confiscated goods and give you the [Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_of_the_Old_Gods "Skyrim:Armor of the Old Gods"), [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots_of_the_Old_Gods "Skyrim:Boots of the Old Gods"), [Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets_of_the_Old_Gods "Skyrim:Gauntlets of the Old Gods"), and [Helmet of the Old Gods](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet_of_the_Old_Gods "Skyrim:Helmet of the Old Gods"). The Forsworn will all equip their own gear and run out. When you follow them through the door, you will emerge into a standoff between the Forsworn and [Thonar Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood"), accompanied by a [Markarth City guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard"). After a short conversation, Madanach and the Forsworn will attack and kill Thonar, then fight their way through the rest of the city guard to the gates. Note that some of the townsfolk may be hostile to the Forsworn and can be killed during the breakout.

Once outside the city walls, Madanach and any remaining Forsworn will then run to [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") where they will take up permanent residence. Madanach's Forsworn at Druadach Redoubt will remain friendly to you if you sided with him, although all other encampments will still be hostile. No matter which approach you used, you will be pardoned.

## Notes

- It is possible to obtain both the Armor of the Old Gods and the Silver-Blood Family Ring.
  - Side with Madanach and stall him in the escape tunnels after receiving the Armor of the Old Gods. When the other Forsworn run outside, you can kill him and loot his key. Head outside and kill the other Forsworn, then return to Madanach's corpse in order to get his note. You can then exit the ruins again and talk to Thonar in order to receive the ring.
  - You can also attack and kill the Forsworn while still in the tunnels. Once you exit, [Thonar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood") will give you the Silver-Blood Family Ring. If Thonar does not approach you to initiate dialogue and give you the ring, the quest may not progress as intended. To fix that, go back to the ruin, then exit to Markarth again. This should trigger Thonar’s approach and allow the quest to finish.
- This quest counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") regardless of whether you choose to help or kill Madanach.
  - Escaping from Cidhna Mine during this quest does **not** add to your "Jail Escapes" statistic, nor will it grant you the [Wanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Wanted#Achievements "Skyrim:Wanted") achievement. It **does**, however, add to your "Times Jailed" statistic.
- You can smuggle your equipment into the jail in advance either by pets, reverse-pickpocketing [Urzoga gra-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzoga_gra-Shugurz "Skyrim:Urzoga gra-Shugurz"), or with the [Secret Servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers#Secret_Servant "Skyrim:Powers") acquired from the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)") *[Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")*.
- Escaping with Madanach and his followers can lead to the unintended deaths of several non-essential NPCs as you make your way through Markarth itself.
  - You can skip to the end of the quest and avoid the potential massacre completely by fast traveling away from Markarth once you've escaped the ruins. You'll need to do this quickly and/or stealthily, before the city guards can become hostile to you and thereby prevent you from fast traveling; you can still complete the quest later by speaking to Madanach after he gets out of the city.
  - Alternatively, wait until midnight before heading out, when most citizens will be indoors and away from the fight.
  - [Vigilant Tyranus](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tyranus "Skyrim:Vigilant Tyranus"), required for the quest [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors"), will never sleep and is always present on the streets of Markarth before his quest is started. He will thus attempt to attack the Forsworn, and as he is essential but weak, he can get stuck in a fight and thus cause the battle to last much longer than necessary. It is advised to begin his quest in order to remove him from the streets.
- The inhabitants of Cidhna Mine are all scripted to die if you decide to kill Madanach in his cell and escape from the mine alone.
- The [Markarth Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Ruins "Skyrim:Markarth Ruins") remain accessible after this quest; however you cannot sneak back into the mine this way as the way back into Madanach's cell is closed off.
- If you side with Madanach, he gives you all your non-quest items at the exit of the ruin. You will receive all your quest items ***after*** Madanach has finished his dialogue with Thonar and started fighting.
  - When your inventory is returned to you, it will include any stolen items that you were carrying when you began the quest. This is unlike going to jail normally, where the guards [permanently confiscate your stolen items](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Stolen_Items "Skyrim:Crime") and do not give them back at the end of your sentence.
  - Once either Madanach or Thonar returns your items to you, the residents of Markarth will act as if you sided with that person in dialogue, regardless of whether or not you killed them after receiving your items.

## Bugs

- If you are doing one of [Delvin's](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") and/or [Vex's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") [special jobs](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), and you trigger this quest before you report back to them, you will be told you failed the Thieves Guild quest when you return to them, because you were arrested.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") fixes this bug.
- Killing the guards in the mine before starting this quest can potentially block quest progression.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Borkul the Beast cannot be intimidated due to the confidence level bug.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, addresses this issue. His confidence value has been lowered one notch to "Brave" instead of "Foolhardy"
- During the quest, Urzoga was supposed to respond differently when you ask about when you will be released; however, the quest stages are set up incorrectly, so the line will never be heard: *"You won't. The Jarl has ordered a life sentence for you. Get comfortable in the dark, 'cause you'll never see the sun again."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Any of the prisoners killed may not get their bodies removed correctly due to their alias in the `DialogueCidhnaMine` quest not getting cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- Some of the Forsworn in Cidhna Mine are not properly killed when siding with Thonar due to still being locked in protected aliases.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.
- If you start the process to escape Cidhna Mine but turn on Madanach while in the ruins, the control quest `MS02EscapeMadanachEnding` is never terminated, which results in Thonar hanging around outside the ruins indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.
  - To fix this, enter `setstage MS02EscapeMadanachEnding 100`
- Thonar's arrival outside the ruins could be delayed due to a control quest checking for the wrong location starting up. The delay was sometimes significant enough that he could be missed entirely and leave the quest stuck.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.
- Getting thrown into Cidhna Mine may disable all sound effects for picking up items or transferring them between inventories. This should turn back to normal after the quest is completed, but can persist even after completion.
- If you kill Madanach and escape by yourself, Thonar may attack you on sight. Due to him still being marked as essential at this point, you won't be able to kill him.
  - To fix this, either cast a [Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") spell on him, or leave the location for 24 and return to the escape exit point. Thonar should be calm and ready to talk.
- You are able to smuggle outside weapons into the prison during the quest. To do this, you must [hotkey](/wiki/Skyrim:Controls "Skyrim:Controls") the equipment before entering the Shrine of Talos. While none of the items will show up in your inventory, they will still appear in the hotkey menu, and can be equipped. However, this only works with quest items, and they may disappear completely afterwards, potentially breaking any of the item-related quests, such as [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") or [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)"). **?**
-  On [PSVR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR") only, the summer 2018 patch (1.4.40.0.8) broke this quest; after submitting to the guards and agreeing to go to jail, you will end up with a black screen almost immediately. You will still hear some audio for a short time, but very quickly you will be unable to bring-up the in-game menu (for Save/Load/Quit), click any buttons or choose any actions, or hear any sounds. Your only option will be to system-close the application. **?**
  - The bug occurs while [Urzoga gra-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzoga_gra-Shugurz "Skyrim:Urzoga gra-Shugurz") is speaking to you. If you load an old save and kill her before starting the quest, the bug should not be triggered, although due to another bug, killing her might lead to you not being able to escape the prison.
  - If you own the game on disk, delete your installation, then re-install the game, but don't apply any patches. Play the game; after you've exited the cell, it should work to save the game, apply all patches, then continue playing.
- While the generic Forsworn at [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") may be non-hostile to you if you side with Madanach, they will still attack animals or other special followers you have with you on sight. This applies to all dogs (including [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas")), the [Dremora Butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler"), and any pets added by Creations, such as the [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)") and [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)"). This is due to these followers not being added to the "[DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction")", unlike the player and other humanoid followers. **?**
  -  Adding them to the [DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction") faction (RefID `E3609`) will fix this problem.

## Quest Stages

| No One Escapes Cidhna Mine (MS02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | I'm imprisoned inside Cidhna Mine, framed for Eltrys' murder. I have to find Madanach, the King in Rags, and clear my name. *Objective 10:* Ask a prisoner about Madanach |
| 10 |  | *Objective 20:* Get past Borkul the Beast |
| 25 |  | *Objective 25:* Talk to Madanach |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Hear Braig's story |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return to Madanach |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Kill Grisvar the Unlucky |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Return to Madanach |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Follow Madanach |
| 100 | ☑ | I have helped Madanach escape Cidhna Mine, and he and his Forsworn have taken credit for all my past crime, clearing my name in the Reach. |
| 200 |  | *Objective 150:* Kill Madanach |
| 210 |  | *Objective 200:* Search Madanach's body |
| 220 |  | *Objective 210:* Read Madanach's note |
| 230 |  | *Objective 220:* Escape Cidhna Mine |
| 250 | ☑ | Thonar Silver-Blood has granted me a pardon for killing Madanach. My name has now been cleared in the Reach. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 55, 75, 77, 80.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS02`.

# Skyrim:No Stone Unturned

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Quest received upon finding the first "Unusual Gem". |
| Location(s): | [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)") |
| Reward: | [Prowler's Profit](/wiki/Skyrim:Prowler%27s_Profit "Skyrim:Prowler's Profit") |
| ID: | TGCrownMisc, TGCrown |
| Suggested Level: | 18 (for the final part) |

The Crown of Barenziah restored

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find one of the 24 "[Unusual Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem")" scattered throughout Skyrim.
2. Become a full member of the Thieves Guild (if not one already).
3. Have the gem appraised by [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") at [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
4. Collect the remaining stones of a full set and return to Vex.
5. Retrieve the Crown of Barenziah and return to Vex.

## Detailed Walkthrough

An Unusual Gem

### What Do We Have Here?

In your travels about Skyrim, you will come upon an ornate jewel (one of twenty-four spread across Skyrim) called an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem#Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"). Subsequent actions after you acquire one of these gems depends on your membership status with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

#### Not a Member of the Thieves Guild

If you are not a member of the Thieves Guild, picking up the first Unusual Gem you encounter will activate the miscellaneous quest objective: *"Bring the Unusual Gem to an appraiser"*.

Depending on your past travels and interactions, following your objective marker will likely take you to [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul"), a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatThief "Skyrim:CombatThief") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). If you have not yet spoken with Maul, he will seek you out with some unsolicited advice. After the conversation, ask him what he knows about the gem. He will tell you that you need to show it to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") of the Thieves Guild, to find out what the gem is worth. Maul will also tell you that to get to Vex, you must first become a member of the Thieves Guild.
If you press for information on the guild, you will be told to find [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf") in Riften's marketplace. You can find him as suggested, or in the [Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") at night. Talking to him will activate the quest [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), which is the first step towards becoming a member of the Guild. Once you have access to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), seek out Vex for her appraisal of the gem. She will tell you that it is one of twenty-four stones that were pried from the [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Crown_of_Barenziah#Crown_of_Barenziah "Skyrim:Crown of Barenziah") of [Queen Barenziah](/wiki/Lore:Barenziah "Lore:Barenziah") by a thief in an attempt to cover his tracks, and that only the complete set of twenty-four stones would be worth anything.
If Maul does not tell you to find Brynjolf, you can seek him out yourself.

#### Already a Member of the Thieves Guild

If you are a full member of the Thieves Guild when you pick up the first stone, the quest is immediately activated with the objective: *"Bring the Unusual Gem to Vex in the Thieves Guild"*. Find Vex in The Ragged Flagon. She will tell you that it is one of twenty-four stones that were pried from the crown of Queen Barenziah by a thief in an attempt to cover his tracks. She will further inform you that the stone is worthless on its own, but that if you can find the other twenty-three, the collection would be worth a substantial sum.

### Finding the Gems

After showing the Unusual Gem to Vex, the gems are renamed "Stones of Barenziah," and will appear as such in your inventory when in your possession. You must now find all twenty-four stones.

You'll need to complete some other tasks before you have access to all locations where the gems are to be found:

- Begin the [Dark Brotherhood questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") or start the [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") quest.
- Purchase [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). (25,000 gold)
- Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") by completing [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons"). You must also start [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") and progress at least to the point where Tolfdir tells you to speak with the Arch-Mage; until this point, the Arch-Mage's Quarters are locked behind an inaccessible door.

Aside from those, most other gems can actually be obtained at any point in the game. Many are located in places that you will be sent to during other quests, so you may want to consider getting the stone concurrently with the quest.

The stones are located in the following places:

| Location | Notes | Related Quest | RefID |

† Will be marked as stolen unless you are of an appropriate faction rank. This doesn't appear to apply to the Special Edition.

### Recovering the Crown

Find the Crown within Tolvald's Cave

Show Vex the full set of Stones, and she will have you travel to [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave") to retrieve the Crown of Barenziah. The cave is three layers deep, and crawling with Falmer, so be sure to prepare yourself. When approaching the crown, three hostile Dunmer Ghosts will appear and attack. After returning with the Crown, you will receive the permanent effect [Prowler's Profit](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems#Prowler.27s_Profit "Skyrim:Gems"), which significantly increases the chance of finding gems in randomized containers.

## Notes

- If you enter Tolvald's Cave without having spoken to Vex about having all the gems, the area where the crown is found will be blocked off by rubble. This will cause you to have to return to Vex and then travel all the way through the cave again to find the crown.
- The gems that will be marked as stolen may say "steal" instead of "take" when acquiring them; in this case, they will still be marked as stolen and if you're caught taking them, you will be reported. This has been partially modified in the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"); see [bugs](#Bugs) for details.
- If your game is prior to [Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") 1.4 and you haven't recovered the stone from within the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), there are multiple workarounds detailed on the location page.
- There are no quest markers for the stones, so unless you intend to find all the stones by chance, it may be best to print out a list of their locations and cross each one off as you find it.
- It is impossible to remove this quest from your list without joining the Thieves Guild; if you don't want to do that, you may be better off ignoring any Unusual Gems you come across, as they have no other use in the game and cannot be removed from your inventory without Vex.
- The stone in the Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary is not generated by the game until either of the related quest lines is started.
- Text in the game code suggests that you were originally supposed to see Tonilia about the gems. The dialogue about buying the gems would have made much more sense in that context.
- Unlike loose gems (such as amethysts, rubies, etc.), the Stones are immovable where they are placed in the environment, so you don't have to worry about them getting knocked off and lost in the game world.
- With the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on, the draugrs in each blue ice deposit at the [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") will have up to 5 gems, usually of flawless quality once the quest is finished.
- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") removes the objective to "Become a full member of the Thieves Guild" from your journal once you speak to Vex about the unusual gems.

## Bugs

- If you gather all 24 stones before getting Vex to identify them it won't advance to the stage where you need to turn them back in to her and your journal will still say to recover the gems (24/24).
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
  -  To fix this, type these console commands: `setobjectivecompleted TGCrown 20 1`, followed by `setstage TGCrown 30`.
- The *Prowler's Profit* may not appear in the Active Effects menu, but it should still be in effect.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- Although the prompt to collect the Unusual Gems says "take" in the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"), NPCs may still report you if you're caught and you'll get a [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") for theft if that is the case. **?**
- The activator script for the Unusual Gems generates a script error and is unable to trigger the theft alarm due to a bad use of linked references. **?**
- Once you've learned that these *Unusual Gems* are actually *Stones of Barenziah* any new stones will no longer stack in your inventory, previously collected stones will stack when presented to Vex however.
- Repeatedly pressing the activate button while picking up a Stone may shortcut this quest. Your inventory will only increase by one Stone, but your quest progress will increase by more than one, allowing you to return to Vex and move onto recovering the Crown before visiting all 24 Stone locations. This is most easily performed with all the words of Slow Time.
  - You can also repeatedly and quickly press the activate button while slowly approaching a gem; this will work if you haven't yet learned a word for the Slow Time shout or haven't yet reached the stage in the main questline where you can learn shouts.
- Sometimes the gems that are supposed to be in [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") and [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") Sanctuary don't appear and will prevent progress with the quest.
  -  Type the following three commands into the console for a workaround: `set TGCrownGemsFound to 24`; `set TGCrownGemsTotal to 24`; `setstage TGCrown 30`. This will not update the journal entry with the correct number of gems found but it will unlock Vex's dialogue to proceed with the quest.
- The finished crown has 25 stones in it, even though only 24 exist. When found without the stones, all 25 of the crown's slots are empty.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- The [Dunmer Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Ghost "Skyrim:Dunmer Ghost") in [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave") may become hostile to each other due to an improper faction setup.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.
- There's a chance only a single male [Dunmer Ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Ghost "Skyrim:Dunmer Ghost") shows up by the crown and that it's not hostile. When talked to, he may say something along the lines of "It's been so many years...", or he may not speak at all. He can also be pickpocketed for an [Elven Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Shield "Skyrim:Elven Shield").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- If you've angered Maul, he will not speak with you about the Unusual Gem, even though he's the quest target.
  - As noted in the text, this can be bypassed by simply joining the Thieves Guild and ignoring Maul.
- You may collect all 24 stones but the journal entry may say you have 23 and only 23 may show in your inventory.

## Quest Stages

| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've found an unusual gem which seems to exhibit magical properties. I should bring it to someone knowledgeable in such goods for appraisal. *Objective 10:* Bring the Unusual Gem to an appraiser |
| 20 |  | With Maul in Riften no longer speaking to me, I'm going to have to continue my search for someone who can identify my unusual gem. *Objective 20:* Find someone who can identify the Unusual Gem |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| No Stone Unturned (TGCrown) | | |
| 5 |  | It was suggested that I show my Unusual Gem to Vex, a member of the Thieves Guild in Riften. However, I'll need to wait until I'm full member of the Guild before she'll be able to assist me. *Objective 5:* Become a full member of the Thieves Guild |
| 10 |  | I've found an unusual gem which seems to exhibit magical properties. I should bring it to Vex at the Thieves Guild for an appraisal. *Objective 10:* Bring the Unusual Gem to Vex in the Thieves Guild |
| 20 |  | The unusual gem has turned out to be one of twenty-four "Stones of Barenziah." According to Vex, they have little value unless the set is complete. *Objective 20:* Recover the Stones of Barenziah (<Global=TGCrownGemsFound>/24) |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Speak to Vex |
| 40 |  | Vex has revealed to me that the Crown of Barenziah is actually a paragon for the Thieves Guild. If I can recover the crown from Tolvald's Cave, she should be able to restore our paragon to its full strength. *Objective 40:* Recover the Crown of Barenziah |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Return to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've brought the Crown of Barenziah back to Vex, who has restored it to its original condition where it now serves as a paragon for the Thieves Guild. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - TGCrownMisc: 0.
  - TGCrown: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGCrownMisc, TGCrown stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGCrownMisc, TGCrown`.
